The City Chamber of Commerce Submits to the Ministry of Finance a Response Regarding the Overlapping Taxation of Native Sugar 103

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce submitted a response to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating that it was responding to an inquiry. It was found that on September 26 of this year, it received Instruction No. 188897 from the Ministry on September 24, ordering it to conduct a thorough investigation of the names, tax rates, standards, commissioned or contracted arrangements, annual tax revenue, whether there was double taxation, and whether the tax regulations had been submitted to the provincial and municipal governments for approval for the collection of native sugar donations and taxes in various provinces and cities, and to report the findings in detail. Upon receiving this order, it was considered that there was no native sugar production in the city, and there was no case to accumulate regarding the taxation situation. Letters were sent to the Shanghai Chaozhou Sugar, Grocery Industry, and Sugar Industry Associations, ordering them to investigate and report on each item in detail. According to the reply from the Chaozhou Sugar and Grocery Industry Association, the association did not know the truth about the taxation of Chaozhou native sugar. Therefore, the situation was forwarded to the Shantou City Native Sugar Industry Association, requesting it to investigate and reply promptly on the various native sugar donation and tax matters inquired about in the Ministry's order. According to the reply, it was stated that the Ministry of Finance, in order to maintain native sugar and revitalize industry, ordered an investigation into the native sugar donation and tax situation in various provinces to provide relief. I respectfully submit the following regarding the obstruction of Chaozhou native sugar production: (1) The collection of native sugar donations in Chaozhou originally existed, but local groups submitted petitions stating that it was a policy that harmed the people and was harsh, and the government approved an order to abolish it. However, Huilai, Jiaoling, and other counties in Chaozhou still have the practice of collecting native sugar transit donations. Whenever native sugar is transported from these counties to Shantou, it is levied under the pretext of local expenses. The amount of each donation is more than 20 yuan per hundred packages. If they are not satisfied with the levy, they will be detained. Local farmers are subjected to this local harsh tax and dare to complain but dare not speak out. How can the weak and small bear this suffering? It is requested that you present this petition to the government to issue an order prohibiting this practice to relieve the people's difficulties. (2) The Guangdong Provincial Property Management Office, under the guise of reviving the countryside and maintaining the sugar industry, implemented native sugar registration, suspended transportation, and purchased sugar, depriving people of their freedom to trade. Various groups in Chaozhou stated that native sugar is the only source of livelihood in Chaozhou, and the rural economy depends on it for maintenance. If transportation and purchasing are suspended, it is no different from driving people to death. They sent telegrams to the constitutional officials, earnestly requesting the abolition. Although improvements have been made, transportation and sales still require licenses and registration. Native sugar is subject to obstruction, the root cause is the impediment to development. Farmers are wary and dare not plant sugarcane, watching famine. In this autumn of rural bankruptcy, when the people are poor and money is exhausted, the impact on local people's lives is unimaginable. It is requested that you present this petition to completely abolish the harsh regulations such as registration and licensing to reassure the people and industry. (3) Chaozhou native sugar is pure and beautiful, with a soft and moist color, sweet and sour, which is completely different from foreign sugar, which has a bright, hard, and clean color. Recently, the Jianghai Customs has regarded the native white sugar transported to Shanghai as having a slight radiance and suspected that it was mixed with foreign sugar. As a result, native white sugar was indiscriminately taxed as foreign sugar, which actually obstructed domestic production. The raw materials of both native and foreign sugar are made from sugarcane, and there is no difference in quality. The only difference is the color due to the different processes of manual and mechanical manufacturing. Chaozhou sugar manufacturing still uses old methods and replaces mechanical manufacturing with manual labor. Therefore, the sugar produced, except for green sugar, which is baked with fire and has no sand or radiance, the remaining white powdered sugar, stick sugar, and red sugar are all made by squeezing cane juice and using soil to remove moisture. After a month, the top end is white sugar, and the bottom end is stick sugar. These sugars all have radiance and sand. The Jianghai Customs does not investigate the quality of the sugar, regardless of the origin, and indiscriminately taxes it as foreign sugar because of the radiance and sand, which is the most unjust thing in the world. It is requested that you present this petition to strictly order the Jianghai Customs to verify the quality of the sugar and not to indiscriminately tax it. (4) Chaozhou red sugar is yellow and of poor quality, and the price is low. According to precedent, the tax was levied on yellow sugar when transported to Shanghai, which is different from the tax rate of Baiji. Recently, the Jianghai Customs has ordered red sugar to pay Baiji tax because the color of red sugar is similar to the standard of No. 11 sugar set by the Ministry, which has increased the tax rate and increased the price. Selling cheap goods at high prices has blocked sales channels. The Jianghai Customs' actions are sufficient to suppress production and impede the opportunity for development, which runs counter to the Ministry of Finance's intention to maintain native sugar. It is requested that you present this petition to strictly order a stop to maintain the sugar industry. (5) Since the opening of the five ports for trade, foreigners have taken the opportunity of the trade treaty to invade the market with foreign sugar. The sales market of native sugar has been deprived, and the livelihood has declined. Fortunately, the government cares about the people's livelihood, increases tariffs, and reduces the surtax. Native sugar can obtain a glimmer of hope. However, in recent years, due to the collapse of the rural economy and the decline in production, it has been restricted by the Guangdong Property Management Office's native sugar registration and transportation licensing, and burdened by transit taxes, resulting in stagnant sales. Foreign sugar takes advantage of the opportunity to import and dump goods, and cannot compete with them. The livelihood of native sugar is becoming increasingly exhausted, profits are leaking out, and the country's economic lifeline is in danger. In order to maintain the national economy and the people's livelihood, it is necessary to exempt native sugar from transit taxes to benefit native products. It is requested that you present this petition to exempt native sugar from transit taxes to close the loopholes. The above-mentioned points are only based on limited knowledge and are respectfully submitted in the letter. I hope that the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce will present this petition to the Ministry of Finance for approval and implementation to maintain agricultural production and benefit the people's livelihood. According to this, it is found that Chaozhou native sugar has been devastated by the heavy taxes and donations imposed by provinces, cities, and local governments over the years. Now that the government is determined to revive the countryside, it is the time when our people are looking forward to revival. Maintaining agricultural production is the key to this matter. In response to the inquiry, the facts are reported respectfully, and it is hoped that you will investigate and submit it to relieve the people's difficulties. According to this, the investigation and reply from the association, although slightly inconsistent with the various items mentioned in the Ministry's statement, the various oppressive situations are contrary to the Ministry's intention to maintain native sugar and investigate and prohibit harsh and miscellaneous taxes. Therefore, the facts are reported respectfully, and it is hoped that you will review and approve the issuance of an order to investigate and prohibit them so that the local native sugar can be developed to be fair.

Declaration of the Reorganization Committee of the Press Industry Union 104

Looking back at our Press Industry Union, it has been established for eight years. In these eight years, we have fought for the revolution and sought the welfare of the masses without any slackness. Although there have been twists and turns and repeated difficulties, our workers have been able to overcome them one after another with a spirit of great fearlessness. It is gratifying to the people of the country, and it is not difficult to imagine the integrity of our union's organization and the rectification of our steps. Now, the workers and others have been promoting the union for several years, and all industry unions have been reorganized according to law. However, our Press Industry Union has been delayed until now and still uses the old name. Although this has nothing to do with the organization of the workers and does not harm their interests, it obviously conflicts with national laws. At this time when the national crisis is becoming more and more urgent, our workers should also be of one heart and one mind, and under the leadership of the party and government organs, strive for national survival and seek the welfare of the workers. We deeply feel the necessity of reorganizing according to law. Therefore, we are now ordered to reorganize and appoint Liu Debao, Hu Ziqi, Ju Zhixiang, Ni Zhengeng, Zhu , Ye Shigen, Zhang Maoguan, Zhang Ruiqing, Yin Xingeng, Wang Fan, Chen Jinrong, Ye Qiming, Ding Zhengchang, Lou Guoxiong, and Lu Shanben as political and theoretical committee members. After receiving the order, we took the oath of office on the 19th of this month. As for the press workers themselves, there will be no changes due to the reorganization, such as the maintenance of the original labor-capital contract, the protection of interests, the self-determination and autonomy of the workers, and we will never rely on others. The strengthening and expansion of the union must be promoted. All these things have been arranged and will not lose any benefits, abolish contracts, or relax the organization due to the reorganization. In the future, all workers will still adhere to the original purpose, work together under the leadership of the reorganization committee, seek the welfare of the society, and strive for the glory of the labor world. This is hereby declared.

Open Letter from the City Anti-Smoking Association to Citizens: Five Key Points for Registration of Smokers; Fellow Countrymen in the Black Sea, Quickly Wake Up! 106

The Central News Agency reported that the Shanghai Anti-Smoking Committee issued an open letter to smokers regarding the registration of smokers: "Fellow countrymen who are sinking in the black sea, it has only been a hundred and several decades since opium harmed China (1840, the 20th year of Daoguang), but the extent of its harm and the depth of its victims have been unimaginable. Since the Republic of China, there have been more poisonous substances such as red pills, morphine, and heroin, which are more fierce and more rampant. If the opium poison of our country is not resolved in one day, the disaster of national subjugation and racial extinction will not wait for others, and we will burn ourselves. The reason why the harm of opium has reached this point is due to the oppression of foreign forces at that time, the help of corrupt officials, treacherous merchants, and unscrupulous people, and the fact that our countrymen are昏瞶recognizing poisonous substances as the supreme峰慰飲鴉to quench thirst cannot be shirked from their responsibilities. The 국민府 government, aware of the fierceness of the opium disaster, promulgated new anti-smoking laws in June of this year. Since then, this city has been actively proceeding based on the six-year policy of complete elimination. This association was established in July to bear the responsibility of坚察督促检举纠王设计调查. At the same time, the government began registering smokers. Up to now, more than 10,000 people have registered, and thousands of people have been admitted to hospitals for smoking cessation. However, judging from the large population of this city and the number of smokers, it can be seen that the number of registered people is only a fraction, and there are many people who are skeptical and watching. Today's registration will end at the end of this month, so the key points are listed in the article to advise: (1) This time, the government has the greatest determination to ban smoking and will eliminate all smoking in the country within six years in stages. It is definitely not the previous policy of '寓禁于'. (2) The registration deadline for smoking bans in this city is mandated to be at the end of the 24th year, and the automatic registration will end at the end of this month. There will be no extension. Compulsory registration will begin in November. (3) This ban on smoking is consistent across the country. Once a smoker loses the opportunity to register, there is no chance to avoid it or register elsewhere, and will be subject to the most severe punishment. (4) The significance of registration is a way for the government to show sympathy for smokers who are old, sick, and deeply addicted. It is by no means a way to诱人register and then force them to quit. (5) If a smoker requests to quit smoking during the registration period, it is also feasible and can go directly to the Public Security Bureau to request completely free treatment. It is hoped that smokers in this city will deeply understand this and quickly register with the Public Security Bureau within these ten days or so. Do not hesitate any longer and fall into the trap of the law."

Two Notices from the Jianghai Customs 108

Tax Reduction for Exported Frozen Ducks; Extension of Ship Tax License

Tang Hai'an, Superintendent of Jianghai Customs, and Ba Guisen, Tax Officer, issued two notices yesterday regarding the extension of the ship tax license period during the suspension period of ships and the tax reduction for exported frozen ducks.

Notice One

It is found that the tax reduction for exported frozen ducks was extended to the end of March of this year in the previous Notice No. 1428 on February 1st of this year. Now, according to the order of the Ministry of Finance, from October 1st of this year to March 31st of the 25th year, all exported frozen ducks should still be taxed at 5% ad valorem. Therefore, we should comply with the order and notify all merchants. This notice is hereby issued.

Notice Two

Regarding the matter of exempting ships from tonnage tax during the suspension period requested by various shipping companies, the Ministry of Finance has ordered the extension of the ship tax license period according to the following rules: (1) Ships that have a legitimate reason to stop sailing at various ports in the country are allowed to extend the ship tax license according to the date of their suspension. However, if the shipowner intends to stop sailing their ship, they must notify the customs in advance, and the suspension period must be at least one month in order to enjoy the benefit of extending the validity period of the ship tax license. (2) Ships that have already stopped sailing, if they have stopped for one month or more, can extend their ship tax license for the number of days. The above two measures apply to both sea and river ships. If the ship tax license of all suspended ships expires during the suspension period, it will be extended according to the number of days from the suspension to the expiration of the license when the ship resumes sailing. All shipping operators are hereby notified. This notice is hereby issued.

Fire at Wulongchi; Two People Burned, One Injured in a Fall; Property Losses Exceed 10,000 109

The Wulongchi Bathhouse at No. 85 Zhejiang Road in the Public Concession caught fire at around 3:30 yesterday morning. The flames spread rapidly and broke through the roof. The fire was like a prairie fire and spread to the two floors of buildings at No. 87 and No. 89 next door. The nearby patrolmen reported the fire to the Central Fire Department by telephone, and the fire trucks rushed to the scene to put out the fire. Because the fire was very strong, it took about two hours to extinguish it. As a result, all the buildings and property of the bathhouse were destroyed. Two waiters were burned while escaping from the fire. One, Ding Qitang, from Nanxun, 26 years old, burned his left arm. The other, Zhang Ahai, 31 years old, injured his hand. A night watchman, Zhang Chubao, from Nanxun, 50 years old, who lived on the street floor, was awakened from his dream after the fire broke out. He panicked and jumped out of the window, injuring himself internally. The firefighters summoned an ambulance and flew him to Baolong Hospital for treatment. During the fire, firefighter No. 371 was burned in his right hand while venturing into the fire. His colleagues also sent him to the工部局hospital for treatment. After the incident, reporters investigated and learned that the losses of Wulongchi exceeded 10,000 yuan. It is said that there was fire insurance.

Amidst the Price Increase of Telephones in This City, the Cost of Calls to England is Reduced by 30%; It is Hoped That the Telephone Company and the Municipal Council Will Pay Attention 110

The New Voice News reported that the Shanghai Telephone Company in the concession, disregarding the difficulties of businesses and ignoring the facts, wanted to increase prices without reason, which aroused the opposition of the entire city. The Municipal Council hired telephone experts from four countries to study the matter in detail, but so far there has been no specific solution. A reporter from the New Voice News, because this matter is related to the interests of the entire city, did not tire of seeking details and inquired from all parties. According to a gentleman who just returned from England, the British telephone authorities, due to the sharp decline in exports and the sluggishness of various industries in recent years, and because industry and commerce have also laid off employees and reduced salaries, implemented a large reduction in the dedicated line business in London City from October 1st of last year. The quarterly fee was reduced from one pound twelve shillings and sixpence to one pound six shillings. The telephone fees in other places, which were previously one pound seven shillings and sixpence, have now been reduced to one pound. The prices of group businesses and business operations have also been reduced accordingly (an average of 30% discount). The loss of the above telephone price reduction was 750,000 pounds in this fiscal year and should be 1.5 million pounds next year. However, it is generally believed that this policy will not only enable the development of telephone services, but also help the prosperity of industry and commerce, and indirectly increase telephone revenue. It is also stipulated that the original price will be restored when the market recovers. It is hoped that the Shanghai Telephone Company, the Municipal Council authorities, and the four-country expert committee will pay attention to this.

Wife of the "King of Flower Associations" Falsely Accuses Someone of Robbery 111

Accusation of Theft Stemmed from Anger at Extortion by Paramour; Sentenced to One Month Imprisonment, Suspended for Two Years

Yu Manman, a Shanghai native and former dancer, and wife of Liu Lianghong, the "King of Flower Associations," shouted "robbery" at 3:55 AM on the 18th of this month near the Xiaorongchang (Little Glory Place) on Dagu Road. When apprehended, she was taken to the Chengdu Road police station. She claimed that a man from Ningbo, whom she knew casually, had robbed her of jewelry and silver worth 289 yuan. However, after investigation by Chinese detective Wang Xichang, it was found that her account did not match the facts, and she was suspected of making a false accusation. She was subsequently prosecuted in the First Special District Court. Because she insisted that she had indeed been robbed, the trial was postponed, and she was granted bail. This was reported in this newspaper. However, because she could not find bail, she remained in custody. Yesterday morning, Judge Liu Yugui continued the interrogation in the Eighth Criminal Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated that, during the postponement, the defendant had made a statement at the police station, claiming that she had an affair with a man from Ningbo nicknamed "Butterfly Flower" four years ago and lived with him for about two months before breaking up. However, this "Butterfly Flower" had forbidden her from having affairs with other men and demanded money from her, and he frequently sought funds from her. On that day, she met him again at the Eight Immortals Bridge and he again borrowed 50 yuan from her, but was unsuccessful. He then took 11.2 yuan in paper money from her wallet. Because she was angry, she shouted "robbery," etc. After obtaining the statement, the police confirmed that there was indeed such a person as "Butterfly Flower" and requested the assistance of the Laozha police station in locating him, but they were unable to find him. Therefore, the defendant's false accusation in this case has been confirmed, and the court should sentence her according to Article 169 of the Criminal Law. However, since the defendant is a woman who acted out of momentary anger, and has expressed remorse, he requested a lighter sentence. He then presented the statement as evidence. When questioned, Wang Manman admitted that the statement was entirely true, and that she committed the act out of anger. She requested leniency. Judge Liu examined the statement and immediately announced the judgment in court: Wang Manman is sentenced to two months imprisonment for false accusation, suspended for two years.

Two Fists Kill a Man 112

Lu Jiarong of Yangzhou Died Buying Sorghum; The Assailant Has Disappeared

Lu Jiarong, a 48-year-old man from Yangzhou, resided at No. 2, Deshun Li, Wu Family Alley, Laiyi Ferry, Pudong. He had long been without steady employment, so he made a living selling hand-rolled cigarettes. Every day, he would set up a stall near the Pang Yutai rice shop at the northern end of Shenxiang Alley Bridge on Pudong Avenue. Next to his stall was Wang Linhai, a local boy (14 years old) who sold sorghum. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, Lu asked Wang to buy a stalk. Wang asked for seven copper coins, but Lu only gave him five. Wang uttered harsh words, and Lu slapped him in the face to vent his anger. At that time, many people were watching. Suddenly, a man, seeing a grown man bullying a child, stepped forward to stand up for the boy. Without asking what had happened, he punched Lu in the chest twice. Lu immediately fell to the ground. The assailant initially thought he was faking it, but then saw Lu's expression change drastically and knew he had caused trouble. He ran away. Lu was still able to speak, so he hired a rickshaw to go to the Yangjiadu police station to request that the assailant be apprehended and investigated. He claimed that the person who had assaulted him had been instigated by the owner of the Pang Yutai rice shop. The police station, seeing that Lu's injuries were serious, immediately ordered him to be taken to the Pudong Hospital for treatment. However, he died en route due to the severity of his injuries. The rickshaw puller, in a panic, left the corpse in front of the rice shop. Afterwards, Lu's wife, Ms. Xu, asked the police station to investigate. The Yang Police Chief brought Wang Linhai, the boy who sold sorghum, and his grandmother, Ms. Shi, to the station. Wang also stated that the person who hit Lu had run away immediately after. The police chief, needing to question the rice shop owner about whether he had instigated the assault, sent for him, but the owner was not in the shop. Only the owner's wife, Ms. Pang Zhang (40 years old), was brought to the station. She denied that her husband had ordered anyone to use force. The police then took the deceased's wife and all the defendants to the District Court for questioning and reported the murder case to the court through the neighborhood chief, Jiang Hongqing, requesting an autopsy to be conducted this morning.

Canadian Mr. Norlin Travels the World; Arrives in Shanghai 114

Experienced Hardships Along the Way; Witnessed Customs of Various Places

According to the Da Mei Evening News, Mr. Norlin, a 25-year-old Canadian, has arrived in Shanghai a few days ago on a grand tour around the world. A year ago, Mr. Norlin was an accountant for an insurance company in Toronto. He then went to his birthplace in Newfoundland and boarded a Norwegian freighter to England. He had previously studied in England. He then took a Russian ship from London to Leningrad, then took a train to Moscow, where he met the late American humorist Mr. Rogers. He then took a train to Kharkov, experiencing hardships along the way. He then saw men and women bathing together, half-naked, at Sevastopol on the Black Sea. He then took a small boat to Eupatoria. When he slipped while boarding the deck, he was fined 25 rubles. He then traveled through Tiflis to the Persian border. Customs officials identified him as a wanderer and blocked his entry. He then presented 500 shares of mining stock, which allowed him entry. He then took a car into Bojing (and) Tehran. Although the road was very flat, he spent the night in a mud house. He then went to the holy city of Meshed. It happened that the King of Persia was visiting the city's Great Mosque. As the King passed, the police ordered passersby to prostrate themselves on the ground to prevent assassination attempts. He then took a car to Quetta in Baluchistan. The car had an armed escort to protect against tribal attacks. He then passed through India, through Delhi, Benares, Calcutta, etc. When he arrived in Chittagong, he was invited to speak at the Law Library. As he was going to the library, gunshots suddenly rang out. Everyone rushed to him, thinking he had been shot. He then bought a bicycle and traveled through Assam to the Khasi Hills, where women ruled and men obeyed. He asked a man why they did not fight for independence. He replied, "There is no need." He then crossed the Manipur state into Burma, passing through forests and carrying his bicycle up and down mountains along muddy roads into Mandalay. At one point he was warned not to buy food from the scholars, because it was their custom to poison those whom they respect, to please the gods. He then entered Siam, where life was better. At night, he could stay in Buddhist temples. He then traveled along the railway line through the Malay Peninsula to Penang and Surabaya, where he lectured at various schools. He then arrived at Segamat in the state of Johor. His bicycle suddenly broke down en route, and he spent the night in a thatched hut in the wilderness, hearing the sounds of beasts. He peeked out and saw a huge tiger in the moonlight. Mr. Norlin stayed in Malaya for three months, then took a boat to Hong Kong and then to Shanghai. He plans to go to North China, Korea, and Japan, and then return to Canada. Mr. Norlin's travel expenses are gradually running out, and he plans to give lectures in Shanghai clubs or schools to raise funds to complete his trip around the world. According to the Zi Lin Bao, Mr. Norlin's travel expenses at the beginning of his journey in April 1934 were less than 100 pounds, which were used up before he reached Singapore. He then raised travel expenses by giving lectures. To date, he has spent less than 500 pounds, and what he has seen and heard cannot be achieved even with a rich traveler's expenditure of 10,000 gold coins. Mr. Norlin plans to travel again after returning to Toronto, but this time as a journalist. Because he has written travelogues for various newspapers during this trip, he already has a wealth of experience in the journalistic profession.

British Merchants Buying Large Quantities; Box Tea Prices Rise by Five Yuan; But This is Due to Market Fluctuations and May Not Last 120

Since the Italo-Abyssinian War broke out, various import and export companies, fearing that the war would be prolonged, have stopped ordering goods. Recently, because the League of Nations decided to impose sanctions on aggressor nations, the situation in Europe has become increasingly tense, with a great sense that war could break out at any moment. Our country's Ping-Shui green tea has always accounted for a large proportion of exports. In recent years, due to the dumping of tea by the Dutch East Indies and Ceylon, most of the European and American markets have been taken over by them. As a result, foreign sales have plummeted. The British merchants Jardine Matheson, Jardine Henderson and other foreign firms in this city, in view of the increasingly tense situation in Europe and the potential for transportation disruptions once the war expands, have been buying large quantities of tens of thousands of boxes in advance. The market price has also risen by five yuan as a result. Moroccan tea merchants are also buying as much as possible, and there is a trend for prices to continue to rise. According to people in the tea industry, this kind of price increase is difficult to sustain and is purely due to market fluctuations.

According to the Shanghai Municipal Council Health Department's September report, the total number of births of foreign residents this month was 91, of whom 77 resided within the Settlement, divided into 37 boys and 40 girls. The Lu Xihou Sues Judge Case Concludes: Judge Yu Changzi Is Found Not Guilty; Lu Requests Withdrawal of Lawsuit, Presiding Judge Does Not Approve; Judge Yu Explains Reasons for Being Accused, Expresses Outrage 125

—Court Verdict: Yu Changzi Not Guilty, Lu Also Forgoes Appeal—

Yu Changzi, a judge in the Civil Division of the Shanghai First Special District Court, has served for four years, known for his integrity and public service, and highly regarded by his superiors. Last winter, the China Industrial Bank, managed by Lu Xihou, collapsed. Lu was arrested by the police on charges of fraud and embezzlement. After preliminary investigation by Qian Hongye, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division of the First Special Court, the court transferred Lu's petition to manage the bank's liquidation to the Civil Division. Judge Yu was assigned to handle the case, and after repeated court sessions,

he summoned parties involving price rights and debts for thorough interrogation. He also appointed an accountant to liquidate all the accounts and once detained Lu in the civil detention center. This summer, Lu sought to reconcile with creditors and drafted a settlement plan, which he submitted to Judge Yu for review. Based on this, a notice was issued to all creditors. However, Lu believed that the settlement terms stated in the notice differed significantly from his original proposal, which he considered detrimental to him. Therefore, he entrusted a lawyer to file a criminal lawsuit against Judge Yu with the First Special Court for falsifying private documents, requesting that he be prosecuted under Article 210 of the Criminal Law (which stipulates that anyone who forges or alters private documents to the detriment of the public or others shall be sentenced to

imprisonment of not more than five years). Wu Zehan, a judge in the Criminal Division, was assigned to handle the case. Last month, during a court session presided over by Judge Wu, Lu Xihou again requested a transfer of jurisdiction, arguing that since the defendant was a current judge of the First Special Court, it would be inappropriate for him to be tried in the same court, and the plaintiff sincerely believed it was inconvenient and could not agree. Therefore, he requested a transfer of jurisdiction, designating another court to handle the case. Judge Wu then suspended the proceedings pending instructions from the higher court. Currently, Lu's request for a transfer of jurisdiction has been rejected, and the First Special Court will continue to handle the case according to law. Judge Wu then

issued subpoenas and sent police officers to serve both parties, scheduling a public hearing at 1:30 PM yesterday in one of the court's courtrooms. When Lu filed the lawsuit, the outside world paid close attention because the defendant was a current judge and the accusation came from someone subjected to judicial interrogation in the court where the judge served. In particular, creditors of the failed bank and the legal community were highly concerned. However, the bank's bankruptcy petition has now been approved by the court, and Lu Xihou has also realized that filing the lawsuit was too hasty. He specifically submitted a request to withdraw the lawsuit, so the atmosphere

suddenly eased. When the court session began, only the plaintiff, the defendant, and Li Jiachuan, the clerk of Judge Yu who was subpoenaed as a witness, appeared. In addition, there were only a few people in the audience. After presiding Judge Wu Zehan and Prosecutor Song Genshan took their seats with the court clerk, Lu Xihou went to the plaintiff's position and stated that the bank had been declared bankrupt by the court, and he requested to withdraw the lawsuit he had filed. Judge Wu stated that under the current criminal procedure law, the lawsuit could not be withdrawn and ordered the hearing to proceed as usual. He then interrogated Li Jiachuan about the procedures for handling the bank's liquidation and issuing the settlement notice. Prosecutor Song then rose and argued that even if the issued

copies and excerpts were not identical, the parties concerned could raise objections in the future, and there was no credible evidence that Lu Hou had suffered any damage. The crime of falsifying private documents was not established at all. The court then questioned Lu about whether he had consulted with his lawyer before filing the lawsuit. Lu admitted that he had consulted with his lawyer, who said that he could file the lawsuit in this way, so he proceeded with the lawsuit. Although the lawsuit was drafted by a lawyer, the draft was prepared by a friend. Then, defendant Yu Changzi stated the process of handling the bank's liquidation and the reasons for Lu's accusation against him, saying that he had been handling the case diligently for several months,

proceeding according to law. Lu knew about the notice of settlement plan that was sent out. The reason why he suddenly sued me was: (1) When I took over the case, I had Lu detained for three days, and he held a grudge in his heart. (2) Because there were 278,000 accounts, Lu asked to be allowed to declare his claims, but I rejected the request as unjustified according to law, so he could not profit from it and abused the lawsuit to intimidate me. Recently, I have received many letters exposing his insider information, so I applied to the president for recusal on August 20. At that time, accountant Li Dinghui came to visit specifically

to persuade me to concede, allowing the declaration of that huge sum of 278,000, and Lu would withdraw his lawsuit against me. I said that I could not be a judge, but I would never break the law, and I refused sternly. Now that Lu is bankrupt, I am unwilling to file a counterclaim against him, but I ask the prosecutor to pay serious attention to Lu Xihou's abuse of lawsuits and false accusations against judges. His attitude while speaking was

extremely agitated, and his anger was evident in his words, moving many who heard him. After Judge Wu finished the interrogation, he immediately announced the verdict, the main text of which stated that Yu Changzi was not guilty, and he said to Lu Xihou, "Based on the evidence you presented, the case cannot be established at all. Although you have submitted a request to withdraw the lawsuit, are you convinced by today's verdict, or do you still need to reserve the right to appeal?" Lu did not hesitate and immediately said, "I forgo the appeal." Therefore, this case can be said to have concluded here.

Lawyers Association Requests Courts to Improve Announcement of Notices 127

The Shanghai Lawyers Association submitted a document yesterday to the various courts in the city, stating, "Regarding the proposal that the main texts of civil and criminal judgments should be posted on the day of the judgment and published in newspapers, members have proposed that the main texts of civil and criminal judgments should be posted on the day of the judgment and published in newspapers the next day, which would be very convenient for the parties involved in the litigation. However, it has recently been found that many courts have failed to post the judgments on the day of the announcement or publish them in the newspapers the next day, which is inconvenient for the parties involved in the litigation. It is requested that this be forwarded to the various courts to pay attention to improving this matter." After a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committee members of the association, it was resolved to submit a request to the various courts that, in the future, in addition to posting the main texts of civil and criminal judgments on the day of the announcement, they should also be published in full in the newspapers the next day to ensure convenience, etc. Therefore, it is reasonable to submit the situation for your approval and implementation, which would be in the public interest.

City Chamber of Commerce Provides Guidance on Stamp Duty Issues for Deposit Slips, etc. 128

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday replied to the Huashang Wax Candle Industry Association and Wenming Bookstore, providing guidance on issues related to stamp duty. The details are recorded separately below.

Deposit Slips

In reply to the Huashang Wax Candle Industry Association, "Your letter of the 17th of this month has been received and noted. The stamp duty for each deposit slip is 2 cents, and the stamp duty for each deposit booklet is 2 jiao per year. For savings deposits, regardless of whether it is a slip or a booklet, the stamp duty is generally 2 cents per item. The legislators have set this distinction in weight to encourage savings, in accordance with the principles of the Stamp Tax Law set by the Central Political Conference. Article 15 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Stamp Tax Law stipulates that only deposit slips issued by savings businesses established in accordance with the Savings Bank Law can be subject to the provisions of Article 9 of the tax rate table. As for other stores, even if they accept savings deposits, they should still affix stamps in accordance with the regulations for deposit slips and cannot apply Article 9. This point must be conveyed to the industry for attention."

Stamp Duty on Stocks

In reply to Kaiming Bookstore, "Your letter of the 17th of this month has been received and noted. The restriction in the remarks column of Articles 16 and 17 of the Stamp Tax Law is because the term 'temporary subscription' has been issued for more than one year, and there are no formal stocks. This subscription certificate is already equivalent to a substitute for formal stocks and has acquired the status of a legal certificate. The one-year time limit in the remarks column is the standard for supplementary stamps, regardless of the reason why stocks have not been issued. Therefore, the two reasons mentioned by your company, the extension of the subscription period and the registration of capital increase, are subject to the above supplementary stamp conditions if the period from the issuance of the subscription certificate has exceeded one year. This is the view of the association. If your company believes that there are still doubts, you may continue to submit letters for research or submit them to the ministry for verification. As for Article 17 of that article, the statement that each item with a total amount of less than 10 yuan is exempt from stamps, not only does the Company Law Article 110 stipulate that those who pay in full at one time can take 10 yuan as one share, so there is no so-called share less than 10 yuan. This article refers to the actually paid shares in installments. However, the amount of each share paid in installments shall not be less than 20 yuan, and the amount payable for the first time shall not be less than one-half of the face value in accordance with Article 96 of the Company Law. Therefore, the shares paid in installments are at least 10 yuan per share, and there is no so-called share less than 10 yuan. Therefore, as your company's theory is that the sentence 'less than 10 yuan is exempt' becomes a formality."

Health Department Reports on Sanitation Conditions in Concessions Last Month 130

According to the Public Concession Health Department's report for September, the number of gastrointestinal diseases this month was significantly lower than in previous years. The reason is probably due to the pure weather last month, which made it difficult for diseases to breed. In normal times, September is actually one of the unhealthy months. Because during the summer heat, flies gather in shady places due to fear of the sun, and their activity is reduced. After the autumn coolness, they come out in droves, so the harm is more intense. Furthermore, autumn diseases in Shanghai are always brought in from other places and are closely related to those who go out to escape the summer heat. The reduction in autumn diseases in this port this year may also be due to changes in the locations where summer vacationers lived this year. In general, the number of autumn diseases that occur varies for different reasons, but September of this year can be considered smooth. In terms of common infectious diseases, those belonging to the digestive system have decreased, while those belonging to the respiratory system have slightly increased. Other diseases that have increased include malaria, which has increased by 45 cases, mostly among residents of the eastern and western districts. One foreign man, aged 28, died of rabies because he did not receive treatment. One foreign man and one Chinese woman, who had only been vaccinated once in their early years and had never been vaccinated in their lives, respectively, were infected with smallpox. Both of them have recovered. Furthermore, during the month of September, a total of 34,674 people were vaccinated against cholera, of which approximately 3,000 were rickshaw pullers registered for vaccination. In addition, 1,8992 people received the second vaccination. This is the end of the cholera vaccination period. Statistics for the entire summer season show that the number of people vaccinated against cholera was 194,331, and the number of people who received the second vaccination was 11,659. These numbers are slightly higher than in previous years, which may be one of the reasons why cholera did not occur in this port this year and gastrointestinal diseases decreased.

On the Way to Ningbo, Another Young Man Jumps into the Sea on the New Ningshao Steamer, Committing Suicide in the Litongsha Waters, Four Suicide Notes with Bitter Words Found 140

The New Ningshao steamer of the Ningshao Shipping Company sailed from Shanghai to Ningbo on the 16th. At 7:00 PM that evening, when the ship was in the Litongsha waters, a young passenger jumped into the sea from the stern of the steerage cabin. The situation is as follows:

Jumping into the Sea: The New Ningshao steamer left port for Ningbo at around 5:00 PM on the 16th. At 7:00 PM that evening, when the ship was passing Litongsha, a young passenger suddenly jumped over the stern balustrade into the sea from the stern of the steerage cabin. At that time, many of the passenger tea servers had not yet gone to sleep. After seeing this, they immediately reported to the purser. However, the ship was traveling very fast, and in an instant, it had sailed far from the place where the person had jumped into the sea, making it impossible to retrieve him.

Four Suicide Notes: Afterwards, four suicide notes were found on the left side of the balustrade. Two were written on postcards, one addressed to Ma Qizhou of the Baoxin Weaving Factory on Chezhan Road and one to Shen Huanmin of the Cuisen Tai Cigarette Factory at Xinzha Bridge. The other two were sealed in envelopes, one addressed to Gu Jingxian of Fumin Road and one to Shen Yuwei of the Shiyongchang Store in Shuanggang, Chongming. Except for those addressed and sealed, which were not opened, the words written on the postcards were bitter, including phrases such as "When a person reaches the end of the road, they reach the edge of the world." After the ship returned to Shanghai from Ningbo, the tea servers delivered and mailed them to the addresses.

Moving Company Truck Overturns into River, Driver and Two Laborers Injured 141

Yesterday at around 1:00 PM, a moving company truck belonging to the Taiping Moving Company at No. 790 Beijing Road overturned into a river next to the road near Sunjia Bridge on Military Industry Road in Zhabei. This was because the road there was rugged and narrow, and the driver was careless. The driver, Xu Yu'en, a 25-year-old from Nantong, and laborers Chen Changbiao, a 42-year-old from Ningbo, and Zhou Yunlong, a 48-year-old from Suzhou, were all seriously injured, with their heads bleeding profusely. One employee and one laborer only got their clothes dirty and were not injured. At the time, villagers saw this and reported it to the police, who dragged everyone out of the truck and helped them ashore. Then, they hired a car to take them to the hospital for treatment. At the same time, the company was notified to send a car to try to pull the truck out of the river, but because the silt at the bottom of the river was too deep, it was not until evening that the truck was pulled out of danger.

French Police Cracked Red Pill Case 145

Lu Jintao, a 41-year-old man from Tongzhou, was walking through the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Route des Soeurs in the French Concession at 12:15 AM yesterday morning when he was spotted by Chinese police officer No. 560 of the Yuepu No. 184 patrol, who found his behavior suspicious. Upon searching him, a packet of red pills was found. He was taken to the Route Petain Police Station, where he confessed to buying them from Yan Maotou (76 years old, from Yangzhou), a boy living in a bungalow in Yangjiasha. The police chief dispatched detective Yin Bingnan to take Lu to the address, where Yan, the boy, and suspects Li Fusheng (29 years old, from Changzhou) and Li Wang (25 years old, from Changzhou) were arrested. Seven hundred and fifty red pills and a set of lamp stems were found on Wang's bed and in the kitchen. They were taken back to the police station. Yesterday, they were brought to the Criminal Division 1 of the Special Court 2, where the police lawyer Yuan Jiahuang explained the case and filed a public prosecution in accordance with the Anti-Smoking Law. When questioned, Lu confessed to buying the pills from Yan. When questioned, Yan Maotou confessed, "My father, Yan Hongzhang, was arrested on April 9 for selling red pills and sentenced to one year of imprisonment, which he is currently serving. These red pills were sent by Ming Hexing. Yesterday, Lu came to my house to smoke red pills for three cents and took away another three cents. After being arrested, when the patrolmen came to arrest me, I panicked and put my red pills on Li Wang's bed." When questioned, Li Wang and Li Fusheng both denied colluding with Yan Maotou to sell red pills. However, Li Fusheng admitted that he often went to smoke red pills without being addicted and just played around. After verification by Judge Wang Juexu, the sentence was reserved. The defendants were returned to custody.

Young Woman Petitions for Divorce Mediation, Reason Being Husband's Abuse and Beating 146

A young Ningbo woman, Zheng Shujun, 22 years old, married Qu Quangen, a local man from Jumen Road outside Ximen, two years ago in September. The couple often had conflicts, and there was no peace at home. Recently, Zheng Shujun retained lawyer Tao Ran to petition the local court's mediation chamber for a divorce. Her only reason was that her husband was born with a violent nature and abused and beat her. Yesterday, Judge Sun Jikang opened the court to summon her. The petitioner Zheng Shujun, accompanied by lawyer Tao, appeared in court and stated that soon after the marriage, the respondent took the one hundred yuan deposit book that I had in the Bank of China, claiming to keep it for safekeeping, but in fact, he squandered it all. He also ordered me to go back to my mother's house to borrow money, but I refused because I found it difficult to speak. Therefore, the respondent hated me to the bone and abused me in every way. In October of last year, I was beaten and seriously injured. At that time, I still tolerated it, hoping he would change. Unexpectedly, the respondent thought that the petitioner was weak and could be bullied. Recently, he had a new love, and he became even more outrageous, saying that he would put me to death. In August of this year, he added fists and feet for no reason and pulled out a sharp knife to carry out murder. At that time, I reported it to the police. In such a situation, the feelings are truly broken. I request permission to divorce and ask for compensation for living expenses, etc. When questioned, the respondent Qu Quangen, 24 years old, a coppersmith by trade, stated that all the things she said were not true. He did not want a divorce and asked to be reconciled. After hearing the statements, the judge believed that the statements differed from each other and that mediation was not possible. He ordered the petitioner to file a formal lawsuit separately.

Public Concession Milk Inspection Overview for September 151

The following is an expansion of the report of the Health Department of the Public Works Department. The average daily milk production in Shanghai in September was 29,176 pounds, the average daily cheese production was 703 pounds, and the average daily cream production was 86 pounds. Last month, five types of milk samples failed the chemical standards of the Health Department, and 67 types failed the bacteriological standards, including 18 types. This month, one type B milk farm license was revoked due to selling unlicensed milk and general unsanitary conditions. One person was fined 65 yuan and sentenced to two months in prison for selling unlicensed milk. This month, ten cows died from anthrax, and only one died from pleuropneumonia. In addition, three died from pulmonary tuberculosis, three died from septic pneumonia, two died from metritis, and 18 died from other diseases. Statistics show that a total of 37 cows died this month. This month, a total of 30 groups of cows were inspected, totaling 635 cows.

The catalog includes: promoting new county administration, the future direction of reforming county administration, discussion on the reform of county administrative organizations, the causes of corruption among Chinese officials and its remedies, discussion on new county administration theory and its institutions and programs, surcharges on land tax and county finance, proposed accounting system for ideal implementation of new county administration, the experimental county movement and the future of county administration, suggestions for new county administration plans, exploration of practical issues in implementing the Baojia system, overview of Jiangning Experimental County and its criticism, the actual achievements of fiscal reform in Lanxi Experimental County, the sayings and doings of five experimental counties, the new spirit of Jiangxi's county administration training, the past and present views of Sichuan's county administration, my views on the improvement of county administration in Zhejiang, the county administration and county chief of new Guangxi, the reform of Yuesheng County Administration, and the actual situation of administration in Linchuan, Jiangxi. In addition, there are also special reports on the famous theories of Yang Yongtai, Xiong Shihui, and Yu Tang on new county administration, and other important appendices. It exposes the theory and implementation plan of the new county administration, all based on the actual situation, in great detail. The first edition is just enough to supply subscribers, and the second edition has already been published and is on the market. It is typeset entirely in imitation Song typeface, which is exceptionally clear. The length is over 400 pages, with over 200,000 words. The selling price is eight jiao. There are many purchasers among county and district staff.

Children's Weekly

Wishing Children to Become Little Philanthropists 162

— Lan Shan

Little friends! Today I come to talk to you about the issue of charity.

Our China is really unfortunate to the extreme. It is either a drought or a flood. When it breaks out, it is not just a matter of one county or one province, but it is easily a matter of ten or eight provinces. Think about it, China only has so many provinces, but those who suffer from disaster account for about two-fifths of them. In these disaster-stricken provinces, almost 100 million people are suffering! They have no place to live, no clothes to wear, and nothing to eat, and they are hungry and cold day and night. Sometimes, because they cannot bear the oppression of hunger and cold, they would rather throw themselves into the rolling torrents, sacrificing their precious and pitiful lives. Those children, who do not know anything, are just crying for hunger and cold. Aren't all these tragic and heartbreaking situations really like hells on earth?

Yes, they are in hell on earth, suffering from unbearable disasters, but you, my dear children, are in heaven! You have not encountered water and drought disasters, and you do not lack the satisfying enjoyment of food, clothing, housing, and transportation. You should be happy. But I deeply hope that you children will think about the many pitiful children who are suffering in the disaster areas while you are happy, and find ways to help them.

There is no other way to help them, but to donate some money or clothes to them within your ability. Look, there is a child in this city named Situ Zupei, who personally brought his candy money, which he had saved up on weekdays, totaling fifteen thousand nine hundred and ninety yuan, to this newspaper office on September 15, and asked this newspaper office to forward it to the flood relief association to help the disaster victims. We feel that Situ is really a respectable and lovely primary school student! He would rather not buy snacks for himself and take this money to help the victims, how comforted he must be in his conscience! I hope that many children will also learn from Situ, save the money they spend on buying candy, and send it to this newspaper office or the flood relief association to do a great deed!

Ji Chang Learns Archery 163

— Wei Bingxin

Whether pursuing education, undertaking tasks, or practicing a skill, if one can be focused and persistent, any difficult job can surely be completed. If you don't believe me, please read the following story.

In ancient times, there was an excellent archer named Gan Ying. His skills were extremely high. No matter what birds or beasts, no matter their size, distance, or height, as long as he could see them, he would never miss. Gan Ying had a disciple named Fei Wei. After Fei Wei practiced for a long time, his skills surpassed Gan Ying's. Fei Wei also had a disciple named Ji Chang. After Ji Chang practiced for a long time, his skills surpassed Fei Wei's.

When Ji Chang first arrived at Fei Wei's place to learn archery, Fei Wei said to him, "If you want to learn archery, you should first train your eyesight. When your eyes are open, no matter what is thrust at you, your eyeballs should not move, and your eyelids should not close. When you have learned this preliminary skill, I will then teach you the technique of drawing the bow and shooting arrows."

Ji Chang returned home and secretly thought about how he could learn the skill that his teacher had mentioned. It so happened that his wife was weaving cloth on a loom, and the bar that moved on the loom and the board that one stepped on beneath the loom moved up and down constantly. Therefore, he thought of a method for training his eyesight. He lay on his back under the loom, with his eyes open, watching the moving bar and board. When the bar and board moved to his eyelashes, he felt some discomfort at first, but after two years, it became second nature, and he didn't feel it at all. Even if a very sharp awl point pricked his eye, his eyeballs would not move, and his eyelids would not close.

Ji Chang learned this skill and happily went to see Fei Wei, thinking that he could now learn the technique of drawing the bow and shooting arrows. Unexpectedly, Fei Wei said to him, "It's too early. You have only learned to keep your eyeballs still and your eyelids from closing. You haven't yet trained your vision. You must make the smallest things appear bigger and the finest things appear clearer. When you have learned this second skill, come see me again."

Ji Chang had no choice but to return home again. After thinking for a while, he came up with a method for training his vision. He took a hair from a cow's tail, tied a flea to it, and hung it by the window. He stared at it with his eyes open all day long. Strangely enough, after ten days, the tiny flea appeared to him to gradually enlarge. In this way, after three years, it looked as big as a cartwheel. At this time, he didn't ask his teacher for instructions. He picked up a very small bow and arrow, aimed at the flea, and with a whoosh, shot it right in the heart.

Then, he went to report to Fei Wei. Fei Wei happily said to him, "Good, you have already learned the secrets of archery. You don't need me to teach you anymore!"

Earthworm 164

— Zhen

Every morning, Min'er often saw mounds of soil piled up on the grass. He felt very strange and went over to see what they were. He saw a small hole next to each mound of soil. He didn't know what kind of animal's hole it was.

"Brother Cong, are those small holes over there ant holes?"

"No, those mounds of soil are not actually soil, but the excretions of earthworms. That hole is the hole made by the earthworm."

"Oh! So it's an earthworm hole. The farmers say that they eat the roots of crops, so they often use them to feed the ducks. Why do nature books say that they are beneficial to crops?"

"The farmers mistakenly believe that they are harmful animals. In fact, they eat the fallen leaves and do not eat crops. They can loosen the soil, making it easier for oxygen and nitrogen in the air to reach the soil. Because plants need these gases to grow, they can gradually turn barren soil into fertile soil."

"Brother Cong, I often see earthworms, but is their structure very complex? Do they have mouths and eyes?"

"Earthworms like to live in moist soil in holes. They have a total of about one hundred and forty segments. The fourteenth, fifteenth, and sixteenth segments are called the clitellum, and their color is very light. The remaining segments are pale red on the ventral side and brown on the dorsal side. How do you know which is the head and which is the tail? The one closer to the clitellum is the head; otherwise, it is the tail. Its mouth is shaped like a valve and is very small; you have to magnify it to see it. However, it has no eyes, but its skin can distinguish the intensity of light. It also has no ears, so its hearing is not sensitive. What's even stranger is that it has no distinction between male and female, so it is hermaphroditic."

"Some people say, 'When earthworms sing, there won't be much rain.' Brother, can earthworms sing?"

"This is just a common saying and is completely untrue. The reason people think earthworms can sing is a misunderstanding. Actually, it's the mole cricket that's calling."

Autumn Insect Variety Show 165

— Junpeng

Half of autumn has already passed, and various autumn insects are extremely active. In a very beautiful garden with luxuriant flowers and plants, a cricket met a textile insect and said, "Time flies so fast! More than half of autumn has already passed. We don't have much time left to live. Why don't we take this opportunity to invite some companions and hold an 'Autumn Insect Variety Show'? Wouldn't that be extremely interesting and fun?" The textile insect said, "I'm very troubled by my work, and I also want to find some happiness. I very much agree. Let's make a plan to put it into practice with some friends tomorrow!" The cricket smiled and said, "Good! Good! We will definitely put it into practice tomorrow."

The next morning, the cricket invited some of its kind, as well as tree crickets, katydids, mole crickets, grasshoppers, etc. The textile insect also invited some, including bagworm moths, dragonflies, cicadas, butterflies, moths, etc. The setting for the show was natural and in a very beautiful garden, so there was no need to decorate it. Therefore, the cricket, textile insect, etc., didn't have to make any effort, and the variety show began at nine o'clock that day. Mantises and ants were guest performers.

Dong! Dong! Dong!... It was nine o'clock. The cricket chirped a few times to indicate that the variety show was about to begin. The guests at the event included earthworms, bees, flies, mosquitoes, centipedes, fireflies, etc. In a moment, only the sound of tree crickets, *de ling, de ling*, playing music could be heard. The venue became quiet. Then, the tree crickets stopped playing, and the jasmines played *de ling, de ling* even more elegantly and pleasingly. At the same time, pairs of beautiful butterflies, dressed in extremely gorgeous clothes, danced up and down in time with the music, as light as swallows, making the audience cheer. After the butterfly dance was over, dragonflies came out to perform aviation techniques, circling left and right in the sky, making various gestures of catching insects, and also inviting several companions to form a triangular formation, like bombing planes, performing even more wonderfully, with non-stop applause. Then, there was an ant race for five hundred meters and one hundred meters, a grasshopper high jump competition, and later, a guest mantis came up to try out a short sword. Next, the cricket performed wrestling. One yellow cricket and one black cricket were all majestic and high-spirited, baring their teeth and drumming their wings, as if facing a formidable enemy, preparing to wrestle. First, the black one attacked the yellow one, then lunged left and right, advancing and retreating, without any clear winner, each chirped once and then stopped. The textile insect spun the yarn back and forth! back and forth! , and the bagworm moth weaved a piece of cloth, and that was it.

Children! What do you think after watching the "Autumn Insect Variety Show"? If it seems familiar to you, you might as well go back and hold an "Autumn Variety Show" too.

Blacksmith 166

— Fire

One day, after Min'er had dinner, he went to the street to buy something. He ran to a blacksmith shop, where three or four blacksmiths were busily working at their trade. Their faces were covered with a lot of black charcoal dust. The sweat on their bodies flowed like rain, and their clothes were extremely filthy. Therefore, Min'er asked them, "Why are your clothes so unclean?" One of the blacksmiths replied, "Although our clothes are unclean, we make great contributions to mankind. Such as the scissors used by seamstresses, the saws and planes used by carpenters, etc., are all products of our blood and sweat."

Min'er felt that what he said made a lot of sense. He also thought that although their profession was humble, their contributions were so great! Children, I hope that when you grow up, you will definitely do things that are beneficial to society and not engage in occupations that are useless to mankind, so that you will not be ashamed of the blacksmiths!

Frog and Archerfish 167

— Yide

A frog in a hot place was standing on the riverbank, croaking and croaking incessantly, self-satisfied. The meaning of its croaking, translated, is: I am a frog, my honor is the word "beneficial insect". I can catch pests and protect the five grains. My contribution is great. Who can compare to me! Who can compare to me!

An "archerfish" heard the frog's croaking and became very impatient. It swam to the surface of the water and said to the frog, "Hey! I already know that you are a frog, a beneficial insect that can catch pests. But do you know me?"

The frog immediately stopped croaking and looked at the "archerfish," answering proudly, "I know you. I know you're just an ordinary fish!"

The archerfish said, "Do you know my name? Do you know my skills?"

The frog still said proudly, "I'm not a zoologist, so how would I know you, an unknown nobody! But I know your skills. You can swim, right? Do you know? I can swim in the water, jump on land, and also catch pests! Please don't talk about your skills!"

The archerfish, hearing this, restrained its anger and replied, "Don't brag! You can catch pests, and I can also catch pests. You are a beneficial insect, so I am a beneficial fish. — Please see my skills!"

At this time, a pest happened to fly over, and the archerfish immediately shot water from its mouth like a fountain, shooting straight up three or four feet, knocking the pest down and swallowing it in one gulp.

The archerfish swallowed the pest and said, "What do you think of my skills? Shouldn't I be called a beneficial fish? But I don't like vanity. Although I shoot pests to eat every day, no one comes to call me a beneficial fish, which is of no concern to me. What I hate most is an arrogant attitude. Now, please leave my sight!" Saying that, it shot water from its mouth again like a fountain, hitting the frog on the head with water. The frog felt wet and painful and hurriedly fled.

Lighting a Lamp Underwater 168

— Guo Shan'ai

Children: When you see this topic, you feel a little suspicious, right? I believe you will definitely say this: How can you light a lamp underwater? If you light a lamp, won't the water put it out! That's right: Water can put out a lamp, but we can use scientific methods to subdue it.

Children: If you want to do this game, you only need to prepare a box of matches, a short candle stub, a glass, a small wooden board slightly larger than the diameter of the glass, and a basin (filled with water). Once you have all the above items, you can start playing. When playing: First, light the candle (the wick should be shortened), and drip some of the wax onto the top of the wooden board to connect the wooden board and the candle. Then, put the wooden board into the basin of water. At this time, you can turn the glass upside down, hold it in your hand, and place it squarely over the candle and the wooden board, and press it into the water. You see, the candle is not only burning in the water as it does outside, but also shows many beautiful glows due to the rippling of the water.

Principle: Air is a "substance" of gas. In the world, no matter where, no matter what substance, as long as there is space, it will penetrate and occupy a considerable "space". When we press the cup into the water, the cup is already full of air. Therefore, the water in the basin cannot enter at all. If the water cannot enter, the lamp can burn as usual in the air in the cup.

(A) Health Education Two...Cleanliness Check 169

Explanation

(1) Mother says: Why are Mei Sheng's clothes always so filthy?

(2) She sees that Lan Sheng's bed is very tidy, while Mei Sheng's bed is very messy.

(3) Lan Sheng takes a bath every morning, while his older brother is still lazily sleeping.

(4) The teacher sees that Mei Sheng's clothes are unclean and gives him detailed instructions.

(5) This prompts Mei Sheng to realize that he also sweeps the floor and wipes the furniture with his younger brother in the morning.

(6) Look, the two brothers walk in step, how neat and clean their clothes are.

The Story of the White Mountain Crow (6) 171

— Xi

While it was talking, I was leaning on one of my wings, propping myself up a little, eating with relish. The turtledove remained motionless, perched there, looking at me with pity. At the same time, it saw that I was very tired, looking around, and it understood that I was extremely thirsty. A drop of rain happened to be dripping on a piece of sea green grass from last night; it gently sipped up this drop of rain with its beak, brought it over, and sent it into my mouth, so fresh and pure. Of course, if I hadn't injured my body, someone with its status would never have treated me this way.

I didn't know what love was at that time, but my heart was beating very fast. I was emotionally moved, with a kind of unspeakable happiness. I looked at the two of them, so beautiful and gentle, waiting on me. I wished I could always have breakfast like this, but everything has an end, and so does a patient's appetite. After I finished breakfast, my strength had long since recovered. In order to satisfy the little magpie's curiosity, I told it my misfortune, as sincerely as I had told the pigeon last night. The magpie listened to me very attentively, and the turtledove showed me its goodwill at all times. But as soon as I talked about not knowing what I was since I was a child, the magpie cried out? "Are you trying to make us laugh? You are a mountain crow! You are a pigeon! Oh! Oh! Neither of those are right, you are a magpie, my dear child, you are indeed a magpie—and a very beautiful magpie." It fanned its wings at me slightly, as if fanning a feather fan.

I replied, "But my countess, it seems to me that my color is very much like a magpie. Please forgive me for being presumptuous, for saying such a thing..."

The magpie hurriedly said, "A Russian breed of magpie, my love, you are a Russian breed of magpie! Don't you know that they are all white? Poor child, how ignorant you are!"

I replied, "Madam, but I was born in an old broken bowl in the Mallee region, how could I turn into a Russian breed of magpie?"

"Ah! Dear heart! You are also a low-blooded type; do you think you are the only one who is like this? Everything is with me here, I will tell you what to do, and you will do as I say; at this moment, I will take you with me to see the best things in this world."

Li Huitang Scores Three Goals, Securing Victory Hong Kong Wins Football Championship Guangdong Loses 1-3 Shanghai Defeats Malaya 3-1 173

Athletics Field Crowded

Yesterday afternoon at 3 o'clock, Hong Kong and Guangdong competed for the football championship. The first game was the third and fourth place final between Malaya and Shanghai. The four teams' athletes tried their skills again, fighting fiercely, and the situation changed dramatically. Jiangwan Road was full of football fans watching the game, and the number of excited people broke the record of the previous day. No less than several thousand school groups came from as far away as Nanjing and Suzhou to watch. Mayor Wu personally traveled around to direct the military police to maintain order. Tickets at all levels had already been sold out in the morning. The grand occasion was unprecedented. As a result, Hong Kong relied on the strength of the football king Li Huitang, who single-handedly scored three goals, defeating Guangdong 3-1 and winning this year's football championship. Malaya also defeated Shanghai 3-1. Shanghai won fourth place in this year's football tournament. Guangdong and Malaya were originally scheduled to play at 9 a.m. today to determine the runner-up, but Guangdong had already announced its withdrawal yesterday and will not play again. Malaya won the runner-up without any effort, and Guangdong was third.

Kicking Away Opportunities: Shanghai Suffers Another Defeat; Misses Second Penalty Kick, Ranked Fourth in Football Competition 174

In the previous day's match between Shanghai and Guangdong, the competition was fierce. Defender Li Ning was injured, and Dai Lin and Li Yichen were criticized for being slow. Therefore, the lineup was changed, with Xu Jingcheng and Jia Youliang as left and right wings, Chen Jiaqiu and Zhong Yongsen as inside forwards, and the young and energetic Sun Jinshun as center forward, leading the team. The team appeared completely refreshed and well-coordinated. Yesterday afternoon at 1 o'clock, Shanghai began the match against Malaya. Chen Jiaqiu, Jia Youliang, and Xu Jingcheng were the most active, but due to bad luck, the Shanghai team had several corner kick opportunities. Chen Jiaqiu's long shots and close attacks were unsuccessful. The Shanghai team's momentum was unstoppable, but the Malayan team's goal became the ultimate target. After 20 minutes of fierce fighting, neither side had scored.

Bad Luck, Wasted Efforts: Shanghai's left winger Xu Jingcheng was the most hardworking, penetrating deep along the side with speed and power, dribbling past the defense line several times. From a distance of more than ten yards from the goal, he powerfully shot, but due to bad luck, the ball missed by inches, wasting his efforts. At the 25th minute, Shanghai won another corner kick. The landing point was excellent. Zhong Yongsen got the ball and powerfully volleyed it towards the goal. Everyone thought it would definitely score, but unexpectedly, the goalkeeper dove and saved it. Thousands of spectators sighed in unison. The battle became even more intense.

Handball Penalty: Malaya Wins the Ball. In the 28th minute, Malayan inside forward Li Yiyao dribbled the ball and passed it to Xie Qingfu. Chen Zhenxiang intercepted the ball, but unfortunately committed a handball foul near the 20-yard line. Xie took the penalty kick, shooting directly at the goal. The ball was as fast as an arrow. Goalkeeper Zhang Rongcai jumped desperately and caught the ball. Unexpectedly, Li Yiyao charged forward. Zhang Rongcai panicked and accidentally released his grip. The ball flew past the goal line, only half a ball over the line. He quickly turned around and slapped it out, but the referee's decision was firm, and Malaya was declared the winner, opening the scoring.

Besieged Unsuccessfully: Morale Dwindles. After losing a goal, the Shanghai team ordered a full-scale counterattack. The five forwards clashed left and right, engaging in close combat, but the front line was shaken. Zhong Yongsen, Chen Jiaqiu, Sun Jinshun, and Xu Jingcheng all had excellent scoring opportunities, but the goalkeeper's experience was abundant and his skills were agile, saving many dangerous shots. Despite the prolonged siege, they were unable to score. The Malayan goal was constantly in a state of crisis, but they were divinely blessed and managed to turn danger into safety. The Shanghai team was extremely tired, and their movements became slow, showing signs of dwindling morale. The first half ended with Malaya winning 1-0.

Two Penalty Kicks, Two Misses. After the break, the teams switched sides and continued the game. The Shanghai team was slightly invigorated after being injected with morphine. Five minutes into the second half, the Shanghai five forwards broke through two lines of defense, and in the ensuing melee, a Malayan defender touched the ball with his hand, resulting in a penalty kick. Sun Jinshun took the penalty, and the crowd cheered, thinking they could equalize the score. Unexpectedly, the ball was kicked weakly and rolled along the ground. The goalkeeper pounced and caught the ball, causing great disappointment. People said Sun Jinshun was selling favors. Less than three minutes later, Shanghai won another penalty kick. Chen Jiaqiu took the kick, shooting powerfully like a cannonball towards the goal, but the goalkeeper lightly caught the ball again. The Shanghai forwards rushed to compete for the ball, but the goalkeeper didn't throw the ball far. Xu Jingcheng took another shot, but it was still unsuccessful. It was truly a doom for Shanghai.

Deng Hua Penalized Again: Another Goal. As the saying goes, misfortunes never come singly. Sure enough, in the 16th minute, Shanghai was also penalized with a penalty kick. Xie Qingfu took the kick, shooting calmly into the net at a 30-degree angle to the horizon, making it 2-0. The outcome was essentially decided. In the 25th minute, the Malayan team took a corner kick. Yao Shenghua passed to Xie Qingfu, who took advantage of the chaos and shot another goal, making it 3-0. The Shanghai team had entered the second stage of "pulmonary consumption" and was in an incurable state.

"Iron Leg" Scores: Prevents a Shutout. The Shanghai team reluctantly continued the game in dejected spirits. Fortunately, in the 27th minute, an opportunity arose. Jia Youliang broke through the encirclement alone and quickly passed to Sun Jinshun in front of the goal. From only five or six yards away, he lightly volleyed the ball into the net, preventing a shutout. Congratulations were in order. After that, the Malayan team's defense became stricter. After prolonged back-and-forth attacks, nothing was gained. Malaya won the second half 2-1. The total score was 3-1. The battle ended with Shen Siliang announcing that Shanghai had won fourth place in the football championship.

More Scoring Opportunities for Shanghai than Malaya. In yesterday's match between Malaya and Shanghai, Shanghai actually had more scoring opportunities than Malaya. In total, there were 25 excellent scoring opportunities throughout the match, but only one goal was scored, which was very undeserved. Malaya had 17 scoring opportunities and scored three goals. Their shooting accuracy was indeed higher than that of the Shanghai team. The Shanghai forwards had more courage than strategy and lacked calmness when dribbling the ball in front of the goal. The failure was inherently their own fault, but their bad luck should also be given some consideration.
