Showing Full Potential: The "King of Football" Scores Three Goals, Long-Range Shots and Close Attacks All Performed Handily, Guangdong Team Managed to Pull Back One Point at the End 175

Yesterday afternoon at 3 o'clock, the final of the Hong Kong and Guangdong football championship was held. The two sides were evenly matched, with exciting plays emerging frequently. The battle was extremely fierce, constantly in a state of suspense. Headers and footwork shifted back and forth in an instant, dazzling the thousands of spectators. Their expressions reflected extreme joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness. The "King of Football," Li Huitang, displayed the same prowess as in his prime, scoring three goals single-handedly. The fans were ecstatic. Goalkeeper Bao Jiaping exhausted all his strength in defense, earning a round of applause. Besides, Hong Kong's left winger Zheng Jiliang and Guangdong's inside forwards Yang Shuiyi and Chen Zhenhe displayed skillful techniques, which were also highly appreciated by the audience.

Long-Range Shot from 20 Yards: "King of Football" Succeeds. At exactly 3 o'clock, the silver whistle blew, and the battle began. To show the importance of the final, Mayor Wu was specially invited to perform the opening kick. The mayor kicked the ball directly towards the Hong Kong side. Li Shaorong caught it squarely and flew forward. The two sides clashed, with attacks going back and forth. The Guangdong team closely marked the "King of Football," giving him few opportunities to be active. At the 55th minute, Li Huitang got the ball. In an instant, he crossed the defense line and powerfully shot, but the angle was slightly off, and the ball went out of bounds. At the 20th minute, Huang Shuikang accidentally handled the ball, resulting in a penalty. The spot was about ten yards from the goal. Li Huitang took the kick. Everyone inside and outside the stadium expected Li to pass to the left wing, but with a loud bang, the ball flew into the net. The Guangdong team was shocked and speechless. All the spectators applauded and cheered wildly, praising the "King of Football's" skills, which were indeed extraordinary. The beauty of his shooting posture, the clarity of the ball entering the net, and the strength of his wrists and feet could only be achieved by the "King of Football."

Goalkeeper's Saves: Great Contribution. The Guangdong team attacked fiercely. Yang Shuiyi, Li Hongqing, and Chen Zhenhe desperately attacked, engaging in several melees in front of the Hong Kong goal. Bao Jiaping dealt with the attacks from left, right, above, and below, using his fists and hands with ease. Hong Kong's victory was due equally to the "King of Football's" scoring and the goalkeeper's defense. At the 30th minute, the Guangdong right winger got the ball inside the defense line and powerfully shot. In a very critical situation, Bao Jiaping dived and slapped the ball out of bounds, forcing a corner kick. The whole stadium cheered wildly, praising him as being even better than the "Iron Gate" Zhou Xianyan. Less than a minute later, the three forwards charged out of the goal with the ball. Bao had already caught it, but the momentum was fierce, and he couldn't avoid being knocked down while holding the ball. He threw the ball out of danger from the gaps in the crowd's feet. He was truly calm in the face of danger and exceptionally intelligent.

Showing Skills Again: Second Triumphant Song. The Guangdong team, hindered by the goalkeeper, could not cross the line, and their offensive gradually weakened. Hong Kong's Cao Guicheng also repeatedly went offside. The battle situation became quiet. At the 40th minute, Hong Kong's Li Zhaorong passed the ball to Li Huitang. Surrounded by enemies on three sides, the "King of Football" used his most agile skills to break through a path. From 15 yards away, he kicked the ball diagonally, and the ball went in again, scoring two goals in a row, singing a second triumphant song. "Long live the King of Football!" The cheers deafened the ears. Later, Zheng Jiliang and Cao Guicheng's long-range shots and close attacks both went out of bounds. The first half of the battle also ended with this, with Hong Kong winning 2-0 and Guangdong losing.

Changing Lineup: Powerless. Hong Kong's Li Guowei was injured midway through the first half and replaced by Yang Benhan, who was still able to fight. During the break, the Guangdong team changed their strategy. Initially, because inside defender Mai Shaohan was injured the day before, Tan Jiangbai was internally transferred to consolidate the defense, and He Zuoxian was appointed as center forward. The attacking power was suddenly weakened. In the second half, Jiang Bai was again appointed as forward, and Xie Kui replaced the defender, taking an offensive stance. However, it was still difficult to overcome the "Iron Gate," and they were unable to reverse the decline. At the beginning of the second half, the Guangdong team came like an overwhelming flood, invading the Hong Kong side's territory. The five forwards took turns charging and attacking, but all failed. In the third minute, Guangdong was awarded a corner kick. Chen Zhenhe kicked the goalkeeper before the ball arrived. The referee blew the whistle to penalize the foul. The ball also went into the net, so it was declared invalid.

"King of Football" Wins Thrice: Overwhelming Momentum. In the sixth minute, Zheng Jiliang got the ball and used his speed to penetrate deep into the enemy territory. The enemy rushed to catch up, and he quickly passed it to Li Huitang. The "King of Football" had been waiting for a long time and would not let go of this opportunity. He dribbled past the enemy camp several times and powerfully shot the ball into the goal. Three wins in three battles. The overwhelming momentum made the Guangdong team lose heart. Not long after, the "King" got the ball and flew towards the goal, but the goalkeeper was prepared. With a loud bang, the ball was caught. This was the first time the "King of Football" had failed.

"Black Coal" Is Brave: Causes Dispute. "Little Black Coal" Chen Zhenhe was the bravest, but he was too reckless. Because of the scramble for the ball, Huang Suanxun waited for the opportunity and had a small dispute. Five or six spectators sitting on the ground below the east command platform suddenly rushed into the stadium, intending to help fight. They were persuaded to stop. Mayor Wu personally inspected the area for a week, and the guards were transferred to maintain order, so nothing happened. The match continued, but both sides' interest in the ball was greatly reduced, and the battle was slowed down.

Mediocre: Pulling Back a Point. In the 25th minute, the Hong Kong team adopted a defensive stance. "Little Black Coal" led the three armies to attack bravely. Goalkeeper Bao also opened the net, and Chen Zhenhe slowly shot the ball in, pulling back the most valuable point and preventing a shutout. At this point, the Hong Kong army became more careful and retreated step by step. The "King of Football" stood by with his hands in his sleeves outside the center line. Once, he broke into Mai's formation and collided with Tan Jiangbai, both falling to the ground. The two old friends helped each other up and smiled. Not long after, the silver whistle sounded, and the battle ended. Hong Kong won the second half 1-1, and the overall score was 3-1. Hong Kong won this year's football championship.

Chen Yuqiong Breaks National Games Record in Women's 200m Breaststroke 177

Also Surpasses Yang Xiuqiong's Time

Yesterday's women's 200m breaststroke preliminary was changed to a final due to the small number of participants. The first place was won by Chen Yuqiong from Guangdong. Chen's time was 3 minutes 38.5 seconds, breaking Yang Xiuqiong's national record of 3 minutes 41.1 seconds, and also breaking the National Games women's swimming exhibition record of 3 minutes 58 seconds. Chen is only 15 years old and achieving this is not easy. Yang Xiuqiong withdrew from the breaststroke preliminary. If Yang had participated, Chen would have faced a big threat. Chen Yuqiong is truly a formidable youngster. In yesterday's race, Chen took the lead from the start and continued straight to the finish line, winning over second place Lin Duli by three meters, second place winning over third place Qu Enzhao also by three meters, and third place winning over fourth place He Wenjin also by three meters, which is quite coincidental. The results are as follows: (1) Chen Yuqiong (Guangdong) 3 minutes 38.5 seconds (breaks National Games record), (2) Lin Duli (Guangdong), (3) Qu Enzhao (Hong Kong), (4) He Wenjin (Beijing), (5) Gao Heyi (Guangdong), (6) Xu Zhenwan (Guangxi).

Chen Yuqiong (left), first place, and Lin Duli (right), second place, breaking the national and Far East records for women's 200m breaststroke (Photographed by International and Wang Kai)

Lin Huijun Wins Men's 100m Backstroke 178

Time: 1 minute 23.3 seconds

The men's 100m backstroke final was held after the 1500m freestyle yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. The champion was Lin Huijun from Malaya. Lin took the lead from the start, followed by Chen Zhenxing. At 60 meters, Chen Zhenxing fell behind, and Shi Jinping and Chen Qiqian followed up. Shi's speed was quite fast, almost catching up to the champion Lin Huijun. Lin increased his speed in the last ten meters, so the others could not catch up. Lin won. Hong Kong's backstroke expert Liu Baoxi arrived in Shanghai yesterday, but because he did not participate in the backstroke preliminary the day before, Liu was not qualified to participate in yesterday's final. If Liu had participated, the national record might have been broken, because Liu is the record holder for the 100m backstroke. The results from yesterday are as follows: (1) Lin Huijun (Malaya), 1 minute 23.5 seconds, (2) Shi Jinping (Guangdong), (3) Chen Qiqian (Hong Kong), (4) Chen Zhenxing (Hong Kong), (5) Guo Zhenheng (Guangdong), (6) Su Tianmo (Guangdong).

Men's Basketball

A Newborn Calf Does Not Fear the Tiger - Hebei Retains Basketball Championship - Nanjing Team Suffers Crushing Defeat - Result: 37 to 45 184

The basketball teams of Nanjing and Hebei held their championship match yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. General opinion beforehand leaned towards Nanjing, boasting such Far Eastern stars as Tang Baokun and Li Zhenzhong, along with the elite of the National Physical Education Military Academy, giving them a stronger hope of winning the championship. Unexpectedly, after a fierce forty-minute battle, Nanjing's mainstay, Li Zhenzhong, was ejected from the field halfway through. The team lost its focus, and was disastrously eliminated by Hebei with a score of 37 to 45. The detailed account of the fierce battle is as follows:

Tang Baokun - A Roar Stuns the Audience - After the referee, Shu Hong, blew the whistle and chose positions, the intense battle between the two armies began. Both sides were cautious, and the score remained untouched for a long time. Li Zhenzhong jumped for the ball in the center circle and passed it to Baokun. Taking three steps as two, Li Shaoshu pounced like a hungry tiger. With a single arm raise, Little Tang opened the scoring. The Wang defender committed a foul while stealing the ball. Wang Youcai scored on the free throw. Subsequently, Li Zhenzhong shot through the center like a white rainbow, lightly lifting his hand to the basket. Wu Wenzhong received Baokun's excellent treatment and also scored successfully. The scoreboard read 10, with Nanjing leading at 8. Hebei urgently called a timeout. After the break, their momentum surged. Ze Baocheng, with his tall stature, made two successful shots under the basket. Wang Hongbin scored a long-range shot. Little Li committed his second foul. The Hebei team caught up, making the score 12 to 13.

Li Zhenzhong - Heartbroken Departure from the Battlefield - As the clouds of war tightened, Little Li turned over and exceeded the score again. Unexpectedly, Li was reported for invading again. The scorekeeper stretched out his hand four times. General Li shook his head and sighed, enduring the pain of leaving the battlefield. The Hebei army seized the opportunity to enter, with Wang Ziheng reporting the first victory, tying the score at 15 each. Xu Zhaoxiong continued to perform meritorious service, leading the score all the way. With no one to block the center, they did as they pleased, going from 20 to 16 to 23 to 17. Tang Baokun's heart was ablaze. He used his skills from years past, making a long-range shot and recovering one point. The Hebei team reciprocated in kind, not yielding an inch. At the end of the first half, Hebei still led with 25 to 20.

Hebei Team - Wins the Championship Trophy - After Zhenzhong left the field, the Nanjing team relied entirely on Baokun alone to support the household, commanding the three armies, and continuing to fight. The Hebei army, holding the ambition to win the championship, refused to give up any ground. After the resumption of the battle, Ze Baocheng added two more points, and both Wangs also scored. They took a lead of 34 to 10. Seeing the situation becoming critical, Tang Baokun, unable to attack, switched to long-range shots. Wu Wenzhong followed suit, and the score gradually caught up. Unexpectedly, Changqing committed a foul, and the Hebei team added two points. Tang made another long-range shot, bringing the score to 41 to 36, with Nanjing only trailing by five points. Just as they were about to catch up, time ran out. After the Hebei team scored a few more points, the gong sounded, and the Hebei army defeated the strong Nanjing team and won the championship trophy.

The War - Unspeakable of Baimen - The main reason for the Nanjing team's failure yesterday was due to Li Zhenzhong's ejection from the field, which caused the team to lose contact. However, the team's slow marching was also one of the main reasons for the failure. While marching requires calmness, excessive calmness is also undesirable. Therefore, although the team held the determination to defend tightly, attack slowly, and resist for a long time, time was limited, and it became an eternal regret. However, Little Tang's superb technique should not be extinguished due to the team's failure. The rest were mediocre, with abnormal attitudes. The Hebei team was known for its speed and strength. The two Wang forwards had excellent coordination, often launching short-range attacks, reporting success upon arrival without hesitation. Liu Baocheng, with his natural stature, took full advantage. The two Li and Luo guards also fulfilled their duties. The forwards benefited greatly from their assistance. If the team seeks further development, it will not be difficult to become a strong Far Eastern team.

Women's Volleyball

Guangdong Team Suffers Another Setback - Women's Volleyball Championship Returns to Shanghai Again - Fierce Competition When Old Enemies Meet - Shanghai Remains Powerful with Calm Play 186

In this Women's Volleyball Championship, as a result of each team's elimination, the old enemies Shanghai and Guangdong met again, and the competition was fierce. As a result, Shanghai won with a score of three to one, holding the championship trophy. Everyone finished the match in smiles. Shanghai's volleyball team, both men's and women's, are all powerful. Are they the heroes of the times? The details of the competition are as follows:

Battle Letters Sent Out - Intent to Kill Immediately Aroused - In this volleyball tournament, the confrontation between Shanghai and Guangdong has long been decided. However, in the semi-finals, Hunan rose up to become the champion, and Hong Kong returned defeated, which was slightly unexpected. However, this was determined by the fate of each person, and there was nothing to be done about it. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the Shanghai and Guangdong teams took the field. The referee, Huang Wenjian, laid down the law in three chapters, agreed on the positions, and then issued the battle letter. Shanghai was not polite. Cheng Hongsheng served the ball, not treating the Guangdong team as guests from afar, and giving them a slight concession, scoring six points in a row. Guangdong's Yang Cha Fen was unwilling to submit and retaliated in kind. Thus, in an instant, a chaotic situation was formed, surpassing the record of Shanghai's Miss with a score of 11 to 8. After changing the field, each had their gains and losses, with no difference. Shanghai's Wang Qian served the ball. Guangdong was winning vigorously and was slightly careless. The situation changed immediately. Tu Qian served very well again. Huang Xingfen coordinated and tossed the ball, and the position was just right. The two wings killed the ball powerfully and succeeded unexpectedly. The score was 21 to 18, and Shanghai won the first game.

Cheering and Encouragement - Guangdong Makes a Draw - On the spectator side, the number of people gathered more and more, each enjoying their enjoyment, cheering endlessly, with throats difficult to be hoarse, and enthusiasm was very high. The female generals of the Shanghai and Guangdong teams had each experienced great battles, and were not moved by color, sound, goods, or profits, but each regarded themselves as strong. The Guangdong team served the ball quickly and fluently. Shanghai also had a counter-attack. Neither side suffered military wounds. The Guangdong masses had a strong sense of localism. When the high ball came, they often indicated the path outside the field, "First row," "Second row," "Third row," giving Guangdong one more consideration opportunity. From then on, they soared straight up, unexpectedly winning with a slight lead of 21 to 16, tying Shanghai to a score of one to one.

Without Stopping the Horses - Shanghai Wins Again - Starting the third game, the Shanghai team, under the wink of Chen, launched a large-scale campaign. Zhang Xiangping and Xingfen had to take care of the front and look after the back. The horse hooves made a clicking sound, and the feet did not stop slightly. Xian Zhuzhu stood alone at the heavy pass, like an iron barrier. Although the Guangdong team had fierce attacks from Yang Yuqiong and Yan Xiurong, they did not see any effect. In the first half, Shanghai had already scored 11 points, while the daughters of Guangzhou only had six points. The momentum was gone, and the audience was not at risk. Who knew that virtuality and reality, advancing and retreating, were originally procedures that should have been on the art of war. The Guangdong team used this move, taking advantage of the Shanghai team's victory and complacency, and they made a single effort, instead taking the lead with 19 to 9. The Shanghai ladies, at this point, regretted their initial carelessness, and immediately cheered up, fighting to the death, so that the central hinterland of Guangdong had no quiet land. After the disaster, they finally cleaned up and Shanghai scored 19, while Guangdong still had only 14. After Yang Yuqiong rose again and killed hard, she only had the upper hand at the end of the crossbow, and could not save the overall situation at all, ending the game at 19 to 21, and Shanghai won.

The Sun Shines on the Eyes - Shanghai's Success - In the fourth game, Guangdong was like a man who could conquer heaven and earth, and if they could win back a game, then there would be a good fight in the future, otherwise where would their fame be buried? Therefore, Bao Yiwei served the ball, and immediately gritted his teeth, preparing to force the four doors. When a ball was shot, it was loud and rewarded the heart, and sure enough, it was a resounding one, winning the first half with a score of 11 to 6. The progress was pressing, and when it was 19 to 15, the Shanghai team used continuous and rapid shooting, passing, and splitting, although they did not use much force, and already blinded the eyes and confused the hands, making the Shanghai team chase to a tie, and the soldiers came to block them, which was very dangerous. As a result, the Guangdong team's sun shot from the west, shining in the eyes, and finally became the Shanghai team's consecutive wins of two points, losing the key point with 21 to 17. The Women's Volleyball Championship was also created by the sun, offering it to Shanghai and continuing to dominate. The score was three to one.

General Observation of Both Sides' Skills - Looking at the two teams' balls in general, Guangdong can attack but not defend, so when they encounter a strong enemy, they will be blocked and fall into a difficult situation. Yan Xiurong and Yang Yuqiong are killing stars, but they are heroes of troubled times, not capable ministers of peaceful times, who can share hardships but cannot enjoy happiness. The three rows lack contact and cannot bear to clean up the mess, which is the biggest reason for their defeat. Shanghai's contact skills are breathtaking, but their killing balls are weak and the method is not good, so the progress is not fast. Although they have won the championship today, it seems that they still need plenty of time to train to kill the ball with force.

The Two Lin and Qiu Generals Strive Hard - Completing the Shanghai Tennis Championship - Java Second, Malaya Third 188

The men's tennis singles final was held yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM. The opponents were Xu Chengji from Java and Qiu Feihai from Shanghai. Qiu is a veteran tennis player, and his skills have been deteriorating due to his old age and weak body. However, the battle yesterday was still passable. His long shots from the baseline posed a great threat to Xu, earning him a lot of applause. As a result, Xu defeated Old Qiu in three straight sets and won the championship. There was also the losers' bracket match between Lin Baohua and Qian Yaobin. Qian forfeited and was ranked fourth. Page 20

A Suggestion for Our Country to Strive to Participate in the 11th World Games 196

- Song Ruhai

The World Games have been around for thirty-eight years since the French male buddy——Mr. Ge Huating painstakingly recovered them in 1896 AD. During these thirty-eight years, they have been held ten times in various European and American countries. Next year——1936 will be the 11th World Games in Berlin, Germany. The German government has been preparing for the Games for three years, and a new sports field has been built outside Berlin, such as swimming pools, gymnasiums, and football fields, all of which have been newly planned and built with extremely new and exquisite designs. In addition, an "Olympic Village" has been built specifically to accommodate athletes and guests from various countries. From this, it can be seen that the German government is extremely thorough in its preparation of venues, facilities, and hospitality for this Games. Each matter and item is assigned to a special commissioner to be responsible for the preparation. According to the report of the American committee participating in the World Games, the equipment of this World Games is more complete and thorough than any previous country. People can't help but admire the German national design and the German people's attitude towards sports in all aspects. It can be seen that they are meticulous in every aspect.

However, among the nations of the world today, no one can deny the strength of the German nation, which is stronger than any other nation. The reason for its strength lies in the fact that men, women, old and young, all pay attention to sports, regarding sports as life, almost as if it were innate. They not only advocate it, implement it, and organize it, but the government also established a national sports department, the highest administrative body in charge of sports, on par with other departments of the country, and assigned senior officials to be responsible for it, controlling the national sports cause. Therefore, the effect is great and fast.

Our country's participation in the World Games started in the 9th Games. Before that, almost no one knew of this name and knew of this event. Even those who knew were very few. At that time, Ruhai happened to be studying in America. Because he had a penchant for sports, he was sent by the National Sports Association to participate as a representative. Later, at the 10th World Games held in the United States, our country officially sent Mr. Liu Changchun to attend and participate. From then on, our country had a considerable understanding of the World Games. Therefore, at this Games, the Ministry of Education and the National Sports Committee resolved to send more athletes to participate in various sports such as football, basketball, track and field, swimming, and weightlifting. It is also a good phenomenon for our country's sports.

However, Ruhai has something he cannot refrain from saying. He sincerely hopes that our government will also follow Germany's approach to sports facilities and establish a sports department, the highest sports administrative body in the country, under the jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan, on an equal footing with departments such as education and internal affairs, and appoint senior officials to preside over it, with special responsibilities, planning, managing, and controlling all sports matters, in order to promote the development of national sports, so as to be effective. Ruhai once read the article "On the Construction of a New Sports Administrative System in Our Country" by Professor Cheng Dengke of the Physical Education Department of Central University in the 12th issue of the 2nd volume of the Diligent Sports Monthly. I think that Mr. Cheng's suggestion to form a National Sports Committee under the three departments of education, training, and internal affairs still needs to be improved. A sports department should be set up directly under the Executive Yuan, equal to other departments, and handled in the same system, similar to the situation in Germany today. Isn't this better than jointly forming a National Sports Committee? At the same time, military leaders such as Shi Youdang set an example by starting from their own advocacy and implementing it themselves, such as Hitler in Germany and Mussolini in Italy. In addition to proposing to the people, they themselves practice labor exercise on a daily basis (such as exercising that is beneficial to the body and mind, such as digging the ground and planting flowers). This is exactly the case. If our country, from top to bottom, can have such a trend, then what is urgently needed today is for the government to select and send national sports experts and those who have a keen interest in sports to visit various European and American countries that focus on sports for reference and careful observation, so as to learn from them. The revival of the nation depends on this.

President Wang Encourages the Athletes of the National Games: The Spirit of Sports and the Work of Saving the Country 197

The original text of President Wang's speech at the reception for the athletes of the National Games on the 14th is recorded below. Chairman, distinguished guests, the 6th National Games have been held for several days since the opening ceremony on National Day. In these few days, whether it is what you see at the venue or what you hear in the broadcast reports, you all say in unison that, judging from the order and discipline of the event, it has improved compared to the previous Games, and judging from the sports achievements of the athletes, it has also improved compared to the previous Games. These improvements are the glory of your efforts and the joy of the people of the country who are concerned about sports. The National Games have been held only six times so far, but there has been progress every time. This not only shows your efforts, but also shows the national people's vigorous promotion of sports. The enthusiastic emotions of hundreds of thousands of spectators have been transmitted to the ears and eyes of thousands of athletes, encouraging you and giving you a lot of courage, knowing that society has infinite expectations and infinite trust in you. You are more aware of the importance of your responsibilities. Originally, sports are something that every individual, every nation, and every country should work together on, especially for us during the national crisis. We regard sports as an important work for saving the country and preserving its existence, and we must work together with even more effort. It is often said that a sound spirit resides in a sound body. For the sake of the soundness of the spirit, this is indeed the case. Even for the body itself, its soundness is also necessary, because all work must be handled with a sound spirit and shouldered with a sound body. For example, in war, there is no need to wear iron armor and hold a big knife anymore, but military actions cannot be tolerated by a weak body. Not only war is like this, but although all machines can replace manual labor, and all means of transportation can be replaced by machines, people who are not physically strong and agile are often unable to use machines and are instead burdened by machines. Therefore, in this world, every individual should not only pay attention to movement in terms of spiritual cultivation in order to maintain the vigor and soundness of the spirit, but also pay attention to movement in terms of physical training, so as to forge an iron-like body, which can be sufficient to bear all things and overcome all difficulties. From this point of view, the significance of sports lies in strengthening the race and strengthening the country, and the single-hole significance of sports during the national crisis lies in strengthening the race and strengthening the country in order to save the country and preserve its existence. The source of the national people's enthusiastic emotions for you lies in this, and the source of your regard for sports as a sacred duty and your efforts to fulfill it also lies in this. Speaking of the work of saving the country and preserving its existence, it not only has a consistent meaning with the work of sports, but also the methods and principles are consistent. To give an example, the essence of sports lies in one's own efforts. Every athlete knows that if he wants to achieve excellent results, he must work hard in practice on weekdays. In the world, there are only people who work hard at ordinary times and fail due to occasional misfortune when they enter the competition temporarily, and there are absolutely no people who do not work hard at ordinary times and win due to occasional luck when they enter the competition temporarily, because entering the competition now is not like entering the competition in the past in the Eight-legged Essay era, which can get lucky like winning the lottery. In addition to showing real skills to do real comparisons in order to obtain fair judgment, there is no other way to save the country and preserve its existence. When two countries meet, they rely entirely on their strength to judge the superior and the inferior and to determine the victory or defeat. Therefore, the number of victories or defeats is not determined during the war, but has already been determined in peacetime. In today's world of the jungle, there is no survival without strength, and no country survives without strength. If you want to avoid destruction, you can only prepare your own strength. One more point of strength prepared is one more point of guarantee for survival. Destruction and non-destruction are determined by whether or not you work hard. To give another example, the essence of sports lies in one's own efforts, and the result of effort is inevitable progress. Every athlete knows that he may not necessarily be able to win if he works hard, but he will definitely be able to make progress if he works hard, because if I work hard myself, others will also work hard themselves, so victory is not necessarily certain. Therefore, every athlete, if he wants to make progress, can only work hard to practice, and can only hope that he will make progress, and does not have to hope that others will go bad.

Sports is like this, and so is the work of saving the country and preserving its existence. Today, those who advocate saving the country and preserving its existence all know that they must lie on firewood and taste gall, and indeed they cannot save the country and preserve its existence without lying on firewood and tasting gall. But lying on firewood and tasting gall can only grasp the work of saving the country and preserving its existence, and there must be progress, but it cannot be said that it will definitely win, because if we lie on firewood and taste gall, others will also lie on firewood and taste gall. King Goujian of Yue lay on firewood and tasted gall, while King Fuchai of Wu embraced Sishi's absurd rumors and lived in pleasure, so King Goujian of Yue would definitely be able to win. If he lay on firewood and tasted gall like the Wu Lord Fuchai, then it cannot be said that King Goujian of Yue would definitely win. Today, the strong in the world are striving to maintain their strong position permanently, and not only that, but they are also striving to keep the weak in a weak position permanently. Then, how dare the weak say that the result of lying on firewood and tasting gall will definitely lead to victory? However, victory is not inevitable, but progress is. We can only strive to make progress every day. It is our great wish to gain victory through progress. Otherwise, we have done our best and exhausted our efforts, and we can look up to the sky without shame and down to earth without regret. This is where the sportsman can rest assured and establish his life, and it is also where the patriot can rest assured and establish his life. To give another example, there is no doubt that the result of effort will inevitably lead to progress. However, is this kind of progress already too late? Taking sports as an example, the National Games have indeed made progress every time, but this kind of progress can only be comforting to the whole country. If we compare the results of our National Games with the results of the Far Eastern Games, then we will have to be ashamed of ourselves. If we go further and compare them with the World Games, then we will be even more behind. The reason for this is that our country's promotion of sports is three or forty years later than others. In these three or four decades, others have already made progress and moved forward, so we look forward to it and hope that we can't catch up. But what can we do? Do we report that we are discouraged? Instead of being discouraged, we should make efforts in time. We only need to examine our own results and know that there is progress in each session to know that if we work hard, there will be progress. Then, our efforts are hopeful and our progress is guaranteed. As long as we work hard, we will have fulfilled our responsibilities. Sports is like this, and so is saving the country. Since the world's transportation, some countries have already become inanimate due to their weakness, and some countries have been stimulated and have made efforts in time, and have already occupied the position of the strong. Our country is not weak and small, nor is it strong. There is a special term for it: weak and big. Because it is big, it is envied by people. Because it is weak, it is slaughtered by people. Now, if we want to turn weakness into strength, and politics, economy, military, and culture are all five or sixty years behind, even if we want to make efforts in time, we have already been overwhelmed. But what can we do except make efforts in time? We dare not say that we can certainly survive if we make efforts, but we dare to say that we will certainly perish if we do not make efforts. Then, we can only make efforts in time, and only make double efforts in time. Let's not talk about the past, we can only make efforts now and make efforts in the future. There are quite a few people who often have two kinds of mentality towards everything from white sports to saving the country and preserving its existence. One is too discouraged, thinking that it is too late to make efforts now. The result of this kind of discouragement will inevitably be self-abandonment, which is absolutely unacceptable. The other is too careless. They do not observe clearly or judge clearly between themselves and others. They are complacent with what they have gained. The result is that they do not measure their strength and eventually insult and destroy themselves, which is also absolutely unacceptable. Today, the first thing we must know is that the national crisis is imminent, and we cannot allow ourselves to slack off even for a moment. The second thing we must know is that things are done by people. We only ask whether we do it or not, and we do not have to ask whether we succeed or not. We must be determined, and we must be persistent in our work. We must make efforts at all times, and we must seek progress at all times. We should view all sports work in this way, and we should also view all work of saving the country in this way. Tonight, I have prepared some small groups to invite you to wish you success in your efforts, progress in your progress, and good health in your bodies. May individuals be strong, groups be strong, and the country and nation be strong. Long live the 6th National Games! Long live the Republic of China!

The National Sports Association Held a Meeting of New Directors Yesterday: Wang Zhengting Still Serves as the President, Shen Siliang is Hired as the Chief Executive Officer 199

The third new board of directors of the Chinese National Sports Association held its first board meeting at the New Asia Restaurant at seven o'clock last night. All the newly elected directors attended. As a result of the election, Wang Zhengting was elected as the Chairman of the Board. It was resolved to hire Shen Siliang as the Secretary-General. Other important motions included rectifying the discipline of athletes and severely punishing those who beat referees, and notifying provinces and cities to organize provincial and municipal sports associations to promote sports together.

Anecdotal Notes from the Venue 202

Shanghai's football and basketball championships have already been lost, so when the third and fourth places were decided yesterday, Li Yichen and Lin Jing from the football team and Lu Zhongen from the basketball team were demoralized and unwilling to play. From the perspective of sportsmanship, it was a bit too much.

When Beijing and Hebei competed for the men's basketball championship, both sides had cheerleader teams, and they were fighting fiercely. The Hebei team said, "Hebei is good, Hebei is good, Hebei basketball is great." The Nanjing team said, "It's nothing, it's nothing." In the past few days, the ball games have been a continuous good show, and the Shanghai fans have had a great time. However, the basketball and football games clashed in time, and there was a sigh that they could not see the whole picture. Those who were more sophisticated watched half of each game.

The wind has not been good these days. Referees were beaten on the volleyball court, and spectators also fought each other on the football field. Yesterday, another beating occurred on the football field. Referees are really having a hard time this year.

The Games will close today, and the athletes from each unit will be returning home. Everyone is packing up in the dormitories, and the scene is very sad.

A glimpse of the crowds watching the football match yesterday.

Odds and Ends 203

Paper Hats Are All the Rage at the Venue

Yesterday's weather was still incredibly hot. Modern girls all used umbrellas to shield themselves from the sun. Men who didn't bring hats would fold newspapers into hats to reduce the sun's intensity. Therefore, self-made paper hats were very popular at the venue, almost ubiquitous.

A Last-Place Finisher Takes It Easy

During yesterday's 1500-meter freestyle race, two athletes in the sixth and ninth lanes seemed to lack some strength. At the 1000-meter mark, they were about 100 meters behind the leader. But these two last-place finishers were in good spirits, continued forward, and often smiled at each other. This was a leisurely swim.

Ningbo Old Woman Says "Truly Hard"

The swimming pool is only 50 meters long, so athletes participating in the 1500-meter race must go back and forth 30 times, which is indeed very difficult. Behind the press box, an old woman from Ningbo said, "It's hard, hard, truly hard. Watching thirty laps, my eyes can't take it."

Girls Waiting in the Sun, How Miserable

Yesterday, the girls held up umbrellas to watch the competition, completely blocking the view of the spectators behind them. Therefore, everyone shouted in unison, "We can't see! Please don't hold up your umbrellas!" The girls had to put away their umbrellas and wait in the sun, how miserable.

Starting Gun Scares Spectators

During the 500-meter race, the starter fired a gun to notify the athletes in the last 50 meters, which scared a spectator in the stands. He said, "Why is the starter aiming at him like that? Bullets are not toys, don't let him get hit."

The King of Football Shows His Power, Fans Cheer

When the Guangdong team's right inside forward fouled, the referee decided to award a free kick. Hong Kong's Li Huitang successfully kicked the ball in from 40 yards away. Li, the king of football, is truly extraordinary. When the ball went into the net, fans cheered, the sound wave was huge. One spectator said, "This really has the majesty of a football emperor."

Sun Da-mao Is Also Proficient in Basketball

Da-mao, is a famous track and field athlete, but he is also very proficient in basketball, so yesterday he sat quietly in the center of the north stand of the basketball hall to watch the game until after the game, when he strolled towards the track and field.

Hebei Cheerleaders Are Colorful

Yesterday was the final match between Nanjing and Hebei men's basketball. Each team had cheerleaders cheering them on, their every move was hilarious. It is said that the Hebei cheerleading team has undergone considerable training. It would have been even more exciting if the main character had come.

Reporter Drives Away the Monks

Yesterday, because of the Hong Kong-Guangdong football final, the number of spectators in the track and field was a new record since the opening. Thousands of students from other provinces also sat on the grass in the field. The press box was also occupied by the audience. When the reporters entered the field at 2 o'clock, there were no seats for them. It was truly a case of the kitchen staff driving away the monks.

Copper Coins Are Bought With Money

Yesterday, during the Hong Kong-Guangdong football final, a group of fans were so engrossed that they lost their minds. When they saw something exciting, they threw copper coins in their hands regardless. Several spectators were hit and bled. The venue announcer, upon learning of this, immediately reported, "Your copper coins are bought with money, please don't throw them around."

Students Still Visited in Large Numbers Yesterday 204

Yesterday, there were still four to five thousand students visiting, such as from Chi Chih University, Zhi Ren Yong Girls' High School, etc. More than 200 students from Zhejiang Provincial Medical and Pharmaceutical College, led by Tang Zhao-yu. Students from Beijing and Provincial Yang Middle School left Shanghai last night.

Athletes from remote provinces such as Xinjiang, Suiyuan, Rehe, and Liaoning have also come to Shanghai to participate. At this time when the country is changing, it is especially inspiring. Sichuan Athletes Soliciting Exhibits 206

To Hold a Sports Exhibition in Sichuan

A letter from the Sichuan delegation to all circles to solicit exhibits: Sirs, We humbly believe that Sichuan, located in the western frontier, with inconvenient transportation, slow cultural development, and backward in sports, has not been valued by the general public. However, under the current international political situation and the revitalization of the nation, it occupies an important position and has been recognized by people at home and abroad. The construction of new Sichuan has already begun, and there has been progress in all aspects. However, due to our own limited capabilities, we hope that celebrities and patriots from all walks of life will provide direct and indirect support, so that the construction of new Sichuan can be completed as soon as possible. This is the sincere hope of our team members. The academic skills of our team members are very immature. This time, we were ordered to represent Sichuan at the National Games in Shanghai, regardless of the gains or losses of medals, the superiority or inferiority of results, the purpose is to show national unity, sincere solidarity, pay attention to observation, and learn from each other's strengths. Therefore, our team is now planning to collect as much as possible the sports achievements and sports equipment of various provinces and cities in the country, so that when we return to Sichuan, we can hold an unprecedentedly grand exhibition in the Chengdu-Chongqing area, and evolve the exhibition into a "Sports Library", so that the people of all circles in Sichuan can have the opportunity to observe and study, as if they were visiting various provinces and cities in person, and attending sports venues in person, which will benefit the people of the country. We sincerely hope that you will grant us your kindness. The standards for the exhibits are: (1) Inscriptions and photos of party and state celebrities and conference officials, (2) Sports books, magazines, and various sports competition rules, etc., (3) Sports publications or sports special issues published by magazines, National Games special issues, and conference publications, etc., (4) Photos, forms, and charts of sports, exercise, martial arts, and construction of venues, (5) Various sports equipment of all sizes, or models and sports clothing, etc. Correspondence address: (1) From now until the 20th (during the conference, please hand it to our team at the conference venue), (2) After October 20th, please send it by air to Liu Shenqi, Education Department of the Sichuan Provincial Government.

Guangdong Female Swimmer Hu Yueying Injured Her Right Foot 207

Guangdong's young female swimmer, Ms. Hu Yueying, is expected by all parties to win a medal this time due to her amazing performances. Unexpectedly, Ms. Hu fell and injured her right foot while walking with her peers on the 16th. She could not walk immediately. Later, her father took her to see a doctor for emergency treatment, and she was able to walk on the 18th, but there was still a slight pain. The brave Ms. Hu still did not want to miss this opportunity and disappoint everyone, and insisted on attending the swimming competition. Her uncle, Zhao Bin, and others tried to dissuade her to no avail, and she still wanted to attend the meeting. Later, the team leader Zhang Zongcheng prevented her from attending the performance because she was young and her foot injury had not healed, and it would be dangerous if she exerted herself. Ms. Hu listened and gave up her right, and was disappointed. Tears welled up in her eyes, and she said that she was ashamed to see the elders of Guangdong. After many people comforted her, she was still unhappy and very frustrated.

Team Leaders and Athletes Talk About the Sports Situation in Border Provinces 208

Xikang According to the reporter's interview with the team leader of Xikang, Ma, the most common sports among the people in Xikang include horse racing, string dancing, bullfighting, and shamanistic rituals. After 1929, Long Shou-xian, the former member of the Xikang Political Affairs Committee, promoted new sports such as track and field and ball games. It has not been promoted for ten years, so there is no achievement to speak of. This is the first time to participate in the National Games. There are a total of eleven athletes. The participating events are all track and field. The strength is of course weak, but the purpose of this trip is not to win medals, but to take this opportunity to observe and learn, as a foundation for promotion.

Mongolia The reporter also met eight Mongolian wrestlers in the martial arts field. They were all burly men. They all wore red-topped melon skin satin hats, leather vests with copper nails, big red silk pants, black leather fast boots, and five-color green ribbons around their necks. The strangeness of the costumes was unprecedented for us. According to Enhe Amur, the team leader of the Mongolian delegation, the wrestlers were newly arrived from Mongolia to perform. They all do not speak Chinese. They usually live as nomads, so their physique is very strong. They are brave and good at fighting, but they are very loyal and honest in dealing with people.

Qinghai According to the Qinghai basketball athletes, Qinghai held a provincial sports meeting once in 1920, but at that time there were only track and field competitions, and the results were not very good. After 1926, there were ball games, but they were limited to schools. In recent years, they have worked hard to promote it, and the public has gradually become interested in basketball. In the past, the most popular sports among the people were mountain climbing and horse racing, especially horse racing, which was held several times a month, and there was a scene of everyone leaving their homes.

Tibet Huang Cishu, the team leader of Tibet, told reporters that our province is located in the northwest and has a low culture. Most of the athletes participating this time are from Tibetan schools. The purpose is only to observe and let the people of the country recognize the flag of Tibet and pay attention to it. The sports in our province are very immature and we will work hard to promote them in the future to make them popular.

Suiyuan The reporter also visited Yuan Chenying, the manager of Suiyuan. According to him, the Suiyuan government has spared no effort to promote sports in recent years. The capital of Suiyuan Province, Guihua, has recently built a large-scale public sports field for the public to practice. Track and field and ball games are also gradually becoming popular among the people. There are a total of 15 athletes participating this time. Except for two people participating in martial arts competitions, the rest are all track and field.

Xinjiang The reporter also met Ying Bicheng, the team leader of the province, in the men's athletes' dormitory. According to him, the people of Xinjiang Province have not yet been enlightened. New sports such as track and field and ball games have not been promoted for more than ten years, so they can only be promoted in schools, and the public has not yet been popularized. The existing sports among the people include swimming, horse riding, throwing stones, and fighting, etc. The techniques are quite exquisite and can show the people's martial spirit everywhere.

The Ministry of Education Sends Personnel to Inspect Primary and Secondary Schools and Compulsory Education in Various Provinces and Cities 212

The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 18th to the education departments of Henan, Shaanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Hunan, Guangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Anhui, Jiangxi, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Shandong, Hebei, Shanxi, and other provinces, and the Social Bureau of Nanjing and Peiping, and the Education Bureau of Shanghai, Tianjin, and Qingdao. The original order briefly stated: "After investigation, the regulations on compulsory education have been promulgated and supervised for implementation, and the central government's subsidy funds have been issued successively. The ministry urgently needs to assess the implementation of the various provinces and cities, and in order to promote the education of primary and secondary schools, personnel are hereby sent to inspect and supervise the progress separately, in addition to assigning personnel to be notified separately. This is to inform you." At the same time, the Kangjian Provincial Construction Committee was informed of this intention. The Ministry of Education ordered the following personnel to inspect primary and secondary schools and compulsory education in various provinces and cities: Director Gu Shusen inspects Zhejiang Province, Director Lei Zhen inspects Jiangsu Province, Inspector Dai Xia inspects Jiangxi Province, Inspector Gu Zhao inspects Henan, Shaanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, and other provinces, Inspector Zhou Bangdao inspects Anhui Province, Inspector and Section Chief Zhong Daozan inspects Shandong Province and Qingdao City, Section Chief Dai Yingguan inspects Hebei, Shanxi, and other provinces, and Beiping, Tianjin, and other cities, Section Chief Wu Yan inspects primary and secondary schools and Zhangwu education in Nanjing, Shanghai, and other cities, and supervises the progress separately.

The Ministry of Education also sent letters to Chen Lijiang to inspect ordinary education, higher education, and compulsory education in Sichuan, Xikang, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces, and Yang Zhensheng to inspect Hubei, Hunan, Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian provinces, and supervise the progress separately.

The Last Day of the National Woodcut Exhibition 214

A Rare Opportunity, Hope Shanghai People Will Visit The Entire Exhibition Will Be Moved to Beijing After Closing

The 6th National Woodcut Exhibition was held in Shanghai. It has been exhibited at the Chinese Art and Craft Society on Ai Yu Xian Road for ten days since Double Ten Festival. It was originally scheduled to close on the 20th. It is said that it will be held in Beijing and Guangdong and will not be postponed. The reporter specially visited yesterday for the last viewing. The exhibition's achievements, the richness of the works, and the wonderful content are unprecedented in Shanghai, which cannot but make people admire and love it. For example, Luo Qingzhen's "Sailing Against the Current", "Herding Home", and "Night Crossing" are all meticulously crafted. Li Hua's "Angry Horse", "Go to the City", and "Mutiny" are all masterpieces of craftsmanship, surpassing even the gods. And Ye Fu's "Big Belly Salt", "Funeral", "Sadness" and other works and Lan Jia's "Rickshaw Puller" and "The Same Faces" all powerfully depict the dark corners of the current society and the dynamics of the times. In this period of international disputes and world transformation, artists can break out of the ivory tower and shout for the public. There are also two brick carvings invented by Ye Fu, which are the most exciting in the entire venue, and the preciousness of ancient woodcuts, representing the brilliance of Eastern classical art, are all rare exhibits. The folk art "Year End" has hundreds of works, collecting products from the north and south, representing the customs and popular interests of various places, which should also be noted by modern people who are shouting for mass language and mass art. The remaining famous works from Germany, Italy, France, Japan, the Soviet Union, and other countries, as well as domestic masterpieces, collected a total of more than 1,000 pieces, all of which are rare treasures in the world. Today is the last day of the exhibition in Shanghai. In this rare opportunity, I hope people in Shanghai will visit.

The Shanghai Society and Reading Club of the China Children's Education Society Held a Meeting 215

Shanghai Hujiang University selects students with better grades in each grade as honorary students every academic year to encourage students to study hard and observe and learn. Section Six: Legal Issues 224

— Jun Hui

The issue of women obtaining equal rights with men in public and private law is also the central issue of the women's movement. For example, women demanding legislative and political rights, property management rights, inheritance rights, marriage and divorce rights, the right for illegitimate children to have paternity acknowledged, and the equal application of laws, etc., have always been the main tenets of the women's movement.

If we want to correctly understand this issue, it is necessary to first understand the nature of law.

Many people believe that law is something that maintains social justice and fairness, but this is only a superficial observation. In reality, law is a tool for a minority to suppress the majority. Bebel has very correctly pointed this out!

The subordinate status between races, classes, and genders must be expressed in the country's laws and politics. A country's laws are a favorable organizational expression for the ruling class. Because women are the oppressed and obedient "sex," their legal status is also such." (Woman and Society)

Looking at history, the laws of the Greek and Roman eras were tools for aristocrats and free people to oppress slaves. The laws of the feudal era were shackles for a few lords and monks to oppress the majority of serfs. Even though laws in capitalist societies have absorbed some so-called democratic spirit, they still become iron whips for a few property owners to control the majority of the propertyless!

Law also reveals its unreasonable original form very clearly on the issue of men and women's social rights! In the traditional male-centered society, the law completely stands on the side of men, calling it "reason" and making women obey it! In other words, law has become a talisman for men to restrain women! Especially in feudal society, women were simply objects. Not only did the law not protect women's rights, but it also made the rights of men to oppress women sacred and absolute! The so-called three obediences and four virtues, and the seven grounds for divorce, although not exactly criminal laws and decrees, are used to deprive women of their rights and make men's rights sacred as absolute moral laws. However, law is not a fixed and unchanging thing; it evolves along with the evolution of society! In detail, if the economic foundation of society changes, then the political and legal superstructure also changes accordingly. In capitalist society, the laws reflecting liberal and democratic ideas are naturally different from the laws of feudal absolutist rule. Acknowledging the rights of women as "individuals" is the fundamental motivation for women demanding equal legal rights with men!

The male-dominated society's recognition of women's "human" rights is by no means accidental, but has a practical social basis. The most important of these is that since the era of factories and handicrafts, women have been able to participate in social production labor like men, fulfilling a major task in the national economy. The women's rights advocacy movement that flourished during the French Revolution also started from the above social basis!

The legal struggle of the women's rights movement was actively implemented in European and American countries from the mid to late 19th century. Especially in the UK and the US, the struggle for women to obtain legislative and political rights became a serious women's riot! As a result, male-dominated society finally recognized the principle of equality between men and women in law! But this is only a recognition of the principle! In reality, the women who can enjoy the legal rights recognized by law are limited to a very small number of upper-class women. As for the majority of working women, they still cannot enjoy any legal grace! They still have to create profits for capitalists under the so-called "free" labor contract! Inheritance rights, political rights, etc., have nothing to do with them!

After the European War, almost all countries in the world that entered the stage of civilization completely recognized women's legal rights. Even in the most backward China, the Kuomintang party platform stipulated various rights for women. As a result, many feminists believed that women could obtain equal legal rights under the capitalist social system, and they believed this was a manifestation of their victory! But in our opinion, this is precisely a manifestation of their illusion. If law is a reflection of economic power, then in a society where economic power is concentrated in the hands of a few men, law can only become the exclusive property of a few men, or a tool for them to use at will! The victory that feminists have won is by no means a victory for the majority of women, but only a victory for a few upper-class women!

Now that the capitalist world is gradually entering the fascist stage, the issue of women's equality in law has suffered a serious blow! Before Hitler came to power in Germany, there were forty-nine female delegates, but after Hitler came to power, he sent them all back to their families. Now it is a purely male parliament! The same is true in Italy, where women are not allowed to participate in political and legal institutions. This tendency is currently flourishing in various capitalist countries. Not only are women's legislative and political rights undergoing fundamental changes, but even women's occupational and labor rights are in danger of being deprived! The women's rights advocates who have been fighting for a century will inevitably feel a sense of "previous efforts being abandoned"!

Finally, we can draw a conclusion: the so-called law is a reflection of the economic foundation of society. In a capitalist society where economic power is concentrated in the hands of a few men, the so-called equal laws for men and women will not exist! Only in a society where there is no economic subordination between people and between men and women can law become an equal and rational contract between people, and can the principle of equality between men and women in law be thoroughly realized!
